=== KA ZAITHA ===
Ka nuntakna ka lungngai a,
khatvei leh Eden huan bang nopna
Khatvei leh keugaw gam bang in vul,
nop leh dah ki gawm
Pasian maipha ka zon hang in,
lungkham haksat-na thuak kha zel ing
Itbaang lo mi ka hi zong maw,
Ka Topa aw, na mai hong seel ken maw!!
Nang tawh hong omkhawm den na Pasian ka hi
Hong cing khial ngei keng ei ka ta,
Keilo, akua muang tuan na hiam?
Na Pasian hiah om ing,
Ka muh loh hang a khut tawh hong len gige,
Ka bah ciang a ang sung hong pom,
Itna a thak hong phawk sak zel,
Ka Zai Tha hong dim kik sak zel
Upna hang ze-etna thuak Zawbah,
Mawh lo pi mawhsakna thuak Zawtah!
Tua te honkhia in a lamsang pa, a kua hituan a hiam?
Bang hang lungkia thaneem ding ka hiam?
Bang hang lamet beisak ding ka hiam?
Topa theihloh kaal a piang om kei,
ka nunna ah thu nei pa Amah hi zaw

A hampha Pasian mite toh kikholh khop liailiai mah

Hampha Pasian mite toh kikholh khop liailiai mah

Pa Pasian aki phat ziahziah

hong om pih veve,

kongpi tawn in pai ding hi

=== VUK A PAKNA MUAL DAWN PAN ===
Key : F
Vuk a pakna mual dawn pan, khang lam leimong dongah;
A mual a guam a zang pan, Tui tung leitung tengah;
A teeng mite khempeuh in, Pasian’ lam khial khin hi;
Tua khialhna kol sut ding-in, Eite hong sam uh hi.
Khua lumna gam sunga nung, Huihvot nuam mahmah a;
Etlawm a tamna gam sung, Mihingte sia khin ta;
Pasian hong hehpihna in, A mawkna suak khin hi;
Lawkite’n mittaw bangin, Sing leh suang bia uh hi.
Vantung khuavak thu theisa, Khuavak ta eite in;
Khuamial sunga mangthang sa, Mite khuavak puakin;
Gamlapi a om mite, Pasian meivak puak ni;
Hotkhiatna thu thei lote lungdamna thu puak ni.
Ama lungdamna thupha, Huih aw va lenpih in;
Mi khempeuh theih ding thupha, Tuipi’n va luan pih in;
Mawhneite tang ding sih thuak, Tuuno A hong pai ding;
I kumpi dingin hong tuak, lungdamna tawh mang ding.

Nop kicing man ngahna.

Dahna kipelhna mun;

Dahna kipelhna mun.

Kisa tawntung ding hi.

=== HONG CIAH KIK LEL DING HI ===
KEY:D

Piakkhiatna le thungetna tawh,
I sep kul hi, Topa in hong deih hi.

=== TOPA LAPTOH ZOMI TE ===

=== HONG PI KHIA IN ===
Seh nel gam sung tui na phul sak, Isreal tung na piak bang in
Zogam keu ah Nun na tui luang sak aw
Zomi te kha dangtak lua in Nun na lam pan pial khin ta ung
Na Kha siang tho hong sawl kik in aw Topa

Na Kha siang tho hong lutpih kik aw Topa
Van a lum leh vamin satawh Isreal te na vak bang in
Zomi te zong nek leh dawn hong pia aw
Nangma sungah nuamsa dingin aneu alian hong huai kim in
It na Pasian nang bek hong muang ung Topa
Kei vapai ning mangthang tekiang, Nong gup na thu tang ko ding in

Ka dah ciang hong nuamsak, A mah- Kei ma lawm.
Zeisu a deihna teng cing hi, Lungkham laitak ka lawm,
Thupha deih in amah zuan leng, A ma’n hong pia nawnnawn,
Ni tang le guah tui hong pia hi, Tuk ciangin an hong la sak hi,
Nitaang, guahtui, le an hong pia, Kei ma lawm.
Zeisu a deihna teng cing hi, A tung ka thu man ding,
Kei tungah hong thuman ka lawm,
Bangci ka nial zo ding,
A-mah zui leng ka khial ngei kei, Sun le zan hong cing khial ngei kei,
Sun le zan in zui-ning a mah, Kei lawm,
Zeisu a deihna teng cing hi, Lawmpha zaw deih tuan keng,
Amah tu in ke’n ka muang a, Muang lai ding sih ma teng,
Hih bang lawm tawh nuntak a nuam,
Bei geilo ding hinna a nuam
Bei ngeilo nuntakna nuam na, Kei ma lawm.
=== JESU ===
Jesu … Jesu … Lamdang Thulakpa,
Vanglian Pasian, Jesu … Jesu …
Khangtawntung i Pa, Nopna Kumpi,
Min khempeuh sang alian zaw, Kumpi Jesu.
Phat ding na kilawm hi,
Biak ding na kilawm hi,
Ki lungtang kong pia hi,
Jesu … Jesu … Jesu …
=== ZION ZAWL LA ===
Ka ngaih in kei aa hi, Kei zong ama’ ahing,
Sun le zan lunggulh ing, Sawl bang heina peuh ah,
Nang loin gua bang ka hing zo diam?
Pheiphung suankhawm banzal hong len in aw.
Na sakmel pallun e, etin ka cim thei lo,
Na tongdam khum zungzung, taang bang ka damna hi,
Simlei ah Nang bang ahoih om kei,
Lungdeih sinthu li bang cinna hi cia.
Cho:
Na kha nuai ah hong seel aw,
Na liim nuai hong belsak aw,
Ka lungdeih nang lo om kei,
Sinlai va bang hong phawng cia,
Nang loin deih cing thei kei,
Vang ngaih Zeisu nang lo.
Ka Kumpipa na hi, Pasian zong na hihi,
Ka Pa zong na hi aa, Ka lawm hoih pen zong na hi,
Zato mangpa, damna mangpa na hi,
Sianmang vontawi, min lianpen To Zeisu.
=== ZUI LAI NING ===

Topa in hong nai laitak ka lau thei kei.

=== ZINGNI SUAK SENSAN TA ===

=== ZING NI SUAK SANGIN A TANGZAW ===
Key : Ab

Na hoihna le na thupina,
La-in ka sasa nuam hi.
Sakkik:

Sun nitang sang tangzaw Nang na hi;

Khuamial le meiilum theng h.
Vangliatna puan tawh kizemin,
Min thanna lukhu khu hi;
Thupha vangliatna le hatna,
A tawntungin na nei hi.
Na migitna lian mahmah a,
Na hehpihna kicing hi;
Na ukna itna tawh dim a,
Kei ading hong bawlsak hi.

Ka nuntakna bei ciangin,
Kum tul kum then Topa mai-ah,
Phatna la ka sa ding hi.
=== ZAWHNA OM HI ===
Key : Ab

Tu’n zawhna ka ngah hi.
Sakkik

=== ZANNI TUNI LE A TAWNTUNG ===

=== ZANGKUAM UNOK PAAK ===
Key : F

Lawmpha Jesuh nei ing.

Amah bek ken mu ingh,
Dam na’ng sian na’ng,
Ka deih teng a sung om hi.
Sakkik

Amah zangkuam unok pak hi
A taang zingsol zong hi,
Kei ading tulsawm tulthen sang hoihzaw hi.
Ka lungkhamna teng la khia in,
Dahna hong puak sak a,
Ze-et hun ciang a muanhuai ka tau sang hi.
Upana sia sak theina khempeuh,
Ken tun ka nusia ta,
Ka sung pan a vangliatna tawh hong kem hi.
Sakkik

A taang zingsol zong hi,

A taang zingsol zong hi,

=== VUUK SANG NGO ZAW ===
Key : Ab
Topa Jesuh aw, kei ka siangtho nuam hi,
Keima lungsim sung nong om tawntung ding hi;
Gal khempeuh nawtkhia in hoih lote paai in,
Nong sawp leh ka ngozaw ding hi, vuuk sangin.
Sakkik
Vuuk sang ka ngo zawk thamna dingin,
Topa aw Nangma sipha tawh hong sawp in.
Topa Jesuh aw, keimah nong sawp siang hi,
Na sipha tawh Nong sawp ciang mawhna bei hi;
Mawhna khempeuh paisan siangtho ngah dingin,
Nong sawp leh ka ngozaw ding hi, vuuk sangin.
Topa Jesuh aw, Na kiang kong thum nuam hi,
Na khut nuai panin ka na ngakngak ding hi;
Upna tawh na si buakna ka mu zo hi,
Nong sawp leh ka ngozaw ding hi, vuuk sangin.
Ngak a thuaknate, Topa in na mu hi,
Lungsim thak ka sung ah nong guansak zo hi;
Topa kiang hong pai khempeuh na nial kei hi,
Nong sawp leh ka ngozaw ding hi, vuuk sangin.
=== VUK A PAKNA MUAL DAWN PAN ===
Key : F
Vuk a pakna mual dawn pan, khang lam leimong dongah;
A mual a guam a zang pan, Tui tung leitung tengah;
A teeng mite khempeuh in, Pasian’ lam khial khin hi;
Tua khialhna kol sut ding-in, Eite hong sam uh hi.
Khua lumna gam sunga nung, Huihvot nuam mahmah a;
Etlawm a tamna gam sung, Mihingte sia khin ta;
Pasian hong hehpihna in, A mawkna suak khin hi;
Lawkite’n mittaw bangin, Sing leh suang bia uh hi.
Vantung khuavak thu theisa, Khuavak ta eite in;
Khuamial sunga mangthang sa, Mite khuavak puakin;
Gamlapi a om mite, Pasian meivak puak ni;
Hotkhiatna thu thei lote lungdamna thu puak ni.
Ama lungdamna thupha, Huih aw va lenpih in;
Mi khempeuh theih ding thupha, Tuipi’n va luan pih in;
Mawhneite tang ding sih thuak, Tuuno A hong pai ding;
I kumpi dingin hong tuak, lungdamna tawh mang ding.
=== VANTUNG SIKONG TUM UN ===
Key : Bb
Vantung siklong tum un! Lungdam ni hi a,
Mawh nei mi khat hong ciahkik ta hi;
Apa’n a ta lampi ah na dawn tuah a,
A taimang a ta a ciahpih hi.
Sakkik

Gawsem tumin nuamna tawh phat hi;
Tatsa mi honpite’n tuipi ging bangin,
Suahtakna lapi sa zuahzuah hi.
Vantung siklong tum un! Lungdam ni hi-a,
Ta taimang tu’n kisangkik ta hi;
A mawhna pan mi khat kihonkhia zo a,
Tatkhiatna ngah mithak hong suak hi.
Vantung siklong tum un! Pawi kham ni hi-a,
Vantung mite’n zawhna la sa hi;
Lungdam thu tangko un, gamla pi dongah,
A manpha mi khat suak thakzo hi.
=== VANTUNG OMNA ===
Key : A

Vantung-ah, I omna ding inn vantung-ah.

=== VANTUNG MITE’N PAIPIH ===
Key : Ab

Topa Pasian ta khat atu hi;

A sih khit ciang a nuam bel ngah hi.
Sakkik
A nopna sungah vantung mite’n paipih,
Vankim lai-ah lasa aw dim hi,
Vantung inn nuam sungah Topa in la hi,
A itte tawh nopna a ngah hi.
Gimna bei-in si leng, bang i piang ding hiam?
Eimah in sin sungah ngaihsun ni;
Leitungah nuntakna vangik pua bang hi,
Dahna khitui luannate om hi.
Jesuh nungzuite in sum a tawm hangin,
Vantung khua-ah om sum lamdang hi;
Ze-et bawlsiatna teng i paisan ding hi,
Nungciang kikhel ding lungdamna hi.

I hun, i siamna i zangkhin ding;
Nasepna a tawm hang za ngahna lian hi,
Singlamteh pua kham lukhu khu ding.

=== VANTUNG MITE LA ===

=== VANTUNG KHUAPIPA TATE ===
Key : Ab
Vantung kumpipa tate,
Na pai la sa un aw;
Hong gum Topa’ van pi tawh,
Phat in ah la sa un aw.
Sakkik

Tanglai mi paina lampi;
Tu lai mi nuam sa un aw,
A sawt lo eite’n mu ding.

Zion khuapi mu dek hi;

=== VANTUNG KHUA OM DING HI ===
Key : Ab
Vantung vanglian hehpihna gam,
Mi siangthote inn a hi;
Ama kiangah om tawntung ni,
Leitung na khempeuh paai ni.
Sakkik
Leitung ni abei ciang in-ah,
Nung ciangin inn nuamah;
Mi siangtho te om na lam-ah,
Vantung khua om ding hi.
Tawntung inn nuam vanglian gamah,
I lawmte tua gam om ding;
Tua inn nuam sung-ah om dingin,
Mi namcin a khawm ding hi.
Hong gupna si pha vanglianpi,
Hehpihna gam teng zelsak;
Hih gal gamah i om lai-in,
Hong hehpihna thu gen ni.
Khattang hih hang pai in gen ni,
Leitung dahna kiam ding hi;
Lungsim deihteng tawntung omna,
Kim takin a om ding hi.
Nidang lai a i kikholhna,
Lung sungah hong suak zel hi;
Hih leitunga I kikhenna,
Dah khitui luanna hi.
=== VANTUNG KHUA I TUNG DING HI ===
Key : C
Jesuh’n an bang hong itna pha,
Lam bang pak zaila sa ni;
Thang van inn tang sau siang nun nuam,
Ei a’ ding ngobang lang hi.
Sakkik
Thangvan dawng i tun ciangin,
Deih teng le lai lung damna ngah ding hi;
Kum khua in la sa ni,
Topa Jesuh i phat ding hi.
Thangvan tuanglam i zuih laitak,
Zaitha tawlna om ding hi;
Hi zong i pai khit ciangin-ah,
Zaitha tawl om lo ding hi.

=== THUNGETNA IN LUNGSIM SUNG A ===

=== THUNGETNA HUN PHA HI ===
Key : Eb

Tua lai-ah va kihel leng, damna zatui hipah.
Sakkik

Tua lai-ah va kihel leng, damna zatui hipah.

Honpa kiangah i dahna khempeuh i puak ciang;
Amah in hong khasiat in, i dahna paikhia pah,
Tua lai-ah va kihel leng, damna zatui hipah.

I thunget thuphate peel lo kingah ding hiveh;
Tua thuphate hanginah, lungkhamna teng beipah,
Tua lai-ah va kihel leng, damna zatui hipah.

Hong it Honpa hong ngai in, Hong ngai in, hong ngai in;
Na ang kong beel liingkawmin, Topa hong honkhia aw;
Ka mawhna hang nong si hi, Nong si hi, nong si hi;
Hong hehpih in nong liah hi, Topa hong honkhia aw.
Sakkik
Hong sang in, Topa aw, Hong dahsak nawn kei ning,
Tu’n thupha hong pia aw, Topa hong honkhia aw.
Ka gitloh hang kong thum hi, kong thum hi, kong thum,
Nuntakna lampi Na hi, Topa hong honkhia aw;
Hehpihna in nget neilo, nget neilo, nget nei lo;
Hehpih huai lua nong sa zo, Topa hong honkhia aw.
Na sisan in hong sawp in, hong sawp in, hong sawp in,
Sisan sungah hong diah in, Topa hong honkhia aw;
Upna bek mawhphelna hi, phelna hi, phelna hi,
Tua upna tawh kong beel hi, Topa hong honkhia aw.
=== SINGLAMTEH AH ===
Key : E
Topa min le Ama thu ah,
Ka maizum ngei kei ding;
Ama thu le A Singlamteh,
Ka pahtawi ngitnget ding.
Sakkik
Singlamteh, Singlamteh,
khuavak ka muh cilna,
Ka lung sunga vangik teng bei khinta;
A thu ka up ciang khua ka mu thei ta,
Tu in ka lung a dam tawntung ta.
Jesuh ka Pasian min ka thei,
Tua min bek hi kei’ muan;
Hong maizum sak ngeilo ding kei,
Lam-etna A hong guan.
Ama thuciam kip tawntung a,
A khutsung ka piak teng;
Amah’n phatak na kem dingta,
Ahun a tun’ mateng.
Tua ciang A Pa Pasian’ mai-ah,
Ka min hong sam ding a;
Jerusalem khua thak sungah,
Omna hong pia ding ta.
=== SIHNA GUNGAL KHAT AH ===
Key : G

Kikhawm ding sihna gun gal-ah;

Sihna gungal khatah.
Sakkik
Sihna gungal khatah, Sihna gungal khatah,
Sihna gungal khatah, I tun ding hong nai ta!
I tun ding hong nai ta, I tun ding hong nai ta,
I tun ding hong nai ta, Sinna gungal khatah.
Dahna hong tung ding ka lau lo,
Upna’n ka mu vantung ka en;
Ka za hi vantung mi’n la sa,
Khitui khempeuh Topa’n nul khin;
Sihna gungal khatah.
A itte tawh kikhop nuamna,
Bang aw ka za ding hiam tua-ah;
Ka lungsim hong vut hong tho sak,
Na dang deihna tau mun mang sak;
Sihna gungal khatah.
Topa hong hilh bang ka zuihna,
Lungdam ka ngah a kicinna;
Khawlngei lo-in ka phat ding hi,
Khitui khempeuh hong nul sak hi;
Sihna gungal khatah.

Lampi hong hilh hi na kalsuan simin,
Hong cing hong kem hong makah
Topa hi, tuidam luan na mun ah hong kha ding hi.
Pasian in hong kem dingnuntak hun sung,
Kuamah neih loh thupha hong pia tawn tung
Hun bei ciang zong nang hong kem lai ding hi
Lungnuam takin a gam hong tun ding hi.
=== PASIAN A MINTHANG HEN ===
Key : Ab
Pasian a minthang hen, na lianpi bawl hi.
Leitung a it manin, A ta hong pia hi;
Mawhna seelna dingin A hinna paai a,
Mi khempeuh lut nading hinna kong hong ta.
Sakkik
Phat ve un! Phat ve un! Leitung teng kizel hen!
Phat ve un! Phat ve un!
Mi khempeuh lungdam hen.
Jesuh’ min suangin a Pa kiang va zuan un;
A bawlsa na lianpi hangin phat ciat un.
A si in hong leizo, tatna kicing khin,
A umte a dingin, Pasian in ciam khin;
Mimawh pen nangawn in Jesuh a up leh,
A mawhna mai ding hi, a up khit phet teh.
Na lianpi hong bawlsak in, ei hong hilh a,
Tapa Jesuh hangin, i lungdam lua ta;
A mai i muh ciangin nuam zaw lai ding hi.
Sangzaw, siangzaw, lianzaw, lungdamzaw ding hi
=== PAI IN SEM IN ===
Key : C
Tapidaw ihmu nawn ke’n
Mi ngah na’ng sep theih lai sem
Khutzep-in ding mawk ding maw?
Topa in thu hong pia leh
Sakkik
Pai in sem ding kipan in
Pai in zong A mangte gum
Khua mialna sung mawh nei mi
Tua pawi ah hong paipih in
Topa min na it ding hiam?
Hong ciamna na um zo diam?
Sapna teng A kiang ngen in,
Hong sapna na nial ding maw?
Na sansa bangin umin,
Hong hilh bangin nungta in;
A ma aa bang hi den in,
Sep na tawh upna lak in
Sing lamteh i puak ding om,
kham lukhu na khuk nop leh,
Thathak tawh ma i sot ding
A hun tom a nite tawm
=== PAI IN LA JESU KIANG GEN IN ===
Key : Ab
Jesuh kiang pai in na mawhna gen in,
Na nuntakna ding Ama thu um in;
Na lungsim vangik hong zangsak ding hi,
Topa en in na mawh hong phel ding hi.
Sakkik
Jesuh kiang pai in, na mawhnate gen in,
Ama lam nga-in na mawh hong phel ding hi;
Jesuh kiang pai in, Ama lam zuan in,
Na mawh gen in, Topa’n hogn phel thei ding hi.

Na mawhna mualcia-in a liat hangin;
Mawhna phel ding hi, nuamna ngah na’ngin,
Topa Jesuh a si luang ciamteh in.

Na lau lohna ding, A ang hong pom ding;

A tawntung nuam in na lungdam ding hi.

A hong pattah manin,
Nu aw nong itna lian

Ei adingin manpha

=== NUNTAKNA KHOMUN ===
Key : Eb
Nuntakna khomun kei, Hong pia’n Topa;
Galilee tuili gei, na hih bangmah;
Ka lungsim vahzo kei, Laisim na tawh;
Nangmah tak ka lungdeih hinna thu aw.
Thuman thutak hong pia’n ka Topa aw,
Khomun na piak bang zia’n, Na thupha tawh
Tua hileh kolteng kia’n, Ka suakta ding
Thuman in hong khahkhia’n,
Ka lungnuam ding.
Kei a’ ding Topa Nang, Nuntak khomun
Keimah ka suahtak nang,
Nangmah Thugun;
Nang tawh vantung luah na’ng,
Nong vaak ding hi;
Hong it sakin thuman, Itna na hi.
Topa aw, Kha Siangtho, Kei hong puak in,
Keima mit khua mu lo, Vak sak dingin;
Na thu thuk Lai Siangtho,
Hong telsak ding; Na thu sung pan Nang,
ko hong musak ding.
=== NUNTAK KIKNA THUPHA ===
Key : G

Na gen ciang ngai nuamsak

Na mai khukdin ciangin

Na minpha thangsak in.

Na itna guang sakin

thuhilh a pha pia a,

zak ciang upna na piang sak ta’n
Nungta kikna thupha

Na minthanna kilangsak in
Ko aa dingin a pha.
=== NUNTAK HUN TOM MAH MAH ===

=== NUNNA HONG PIA’N PASIAN ===
Key : F

Nang bawl bang bawl dingin,

Hinna thak hong guan in.

Ka lungsiim sian’ dongin;

Nang tawh omkhawm dingin.
=== NUNGTA AHIH MAN ===
Key : A
Pasian in ah, A Tapa hong sawl
Hong it ding leh hong damsak ding
Ka mawhnate maisak ding hong pai
Amah nungta ahih man ka nunna’n man nei.
Sakkik

Phamawh sa keng, zong lau beek keng
Mai lam hunte a khut sung om cih thei ing
Amah nungta ahih man ka nunna’n man nei.
Naungekte zong Aman hong kepsak
Bangzah takin lungdam huai hiam?
Tua sangin zong lungdam huai zawlai
Nungta ahih manin ahan guak bek om hi.
Ni khatni ciang sihna gungal ah
Haksa pi-in ka kan ding hi
Tua ni ciangin sihna zozo-in
Amah Kumpi ahih lam ka mu thei ding hi.
=== NUNG CIANGIN I ZO DING HI ===
Key : G

I mai-ah koih khin zo hi,

Dam takin Topa’n hong sam, Hong nai hi.

Nung ciang a kiang kimu ding, Nung ciang a kiang kimu ding,
Nung cianga Topa Jesuh tawh mang ding hi.

I tun nading inn nuam ah,

Vantung pan Tua ciang kikhen nawn lo ding,
Lawp a i lam-etna bang,
Upna bangin khial lo-in, Hong nai hi.

=== NITAK THUNGETNA ===
Key : Bb
Topa aw, ko ihmut ma-in, nitak thupha hong pia in;
Mawhna le kisapna ko nei,
Nong hon thei, nong damsak thei.
Siatna in hong kimkot hangin,
thaltang tawh hong kap hangin;

Nong nai ciang ka lau kei hi.

=== NISIMIN NAI SIMIN ===
Key : Ab

=== NI THUM NA GAL-AH ===
Key : Eb
Ni tumna gal-ah, Aw a nuam zingsang,
Topa hong om ciang, Vantung hi zo;
Khualzin na bei in, minthanna mu ding;
Ni tumna gal-ah, Lei bei ni ciang.
Ni tumna gal-ah, Meii kai ngeilohna,
Huihpi om nawn lo, Launa bei ta;
Aw lungdam na ni, Aw bei ngei lo ni,
Ni tumna galna gal-ah, tawntung nopna.

A tungsa i it, i lawmte tawh;

Ni tumna gal-ah, a tawntung ah.
=== NI TAMPI KHENG ZOTA HI ===

=== NI KHAT ===
Key : Db
Ni khat, Ama min phatna van dim napi’n,
Leitung ah mawhna zan bang mial manin;
Nungak sung suakin, Jesuh hong pai suk in,
Mi lak hong teng hi, lampha lak dingin.
Sakkik
Nungta-in hong it, si-in hong hon hi,
Kivui-in ka mawhna a puakhia hi;
Thokik in hong diksak, khawnkhong tawntung hi,
Lungdam huai bel hi, hong paikik ding ni!
Ni khat, Kalvary mual kahto sak uh a,
Singtung kilhcip uh khailum dinginah;
Mawhna teng pua in, simmawh, bawlsiat, huatna,
Nakpi thuaksak uh hi, kei hong Tanpa.
Ni khat, huan sung ah Amah kinusia a,
Ni khat, thuakna tawh pengin tawlnga a;
Vantung mite in, a han hong cingsuk a,
Lam-et bei mite’ muan kei hong hon Pa.
Ni khat, Amah han in siin zo nawnlo a,
Han kong vangkhakna suangpi tukkhia a;
Sihna zo gawpin, sihna pan thokik a,
Tu’n vantung kahzo, tawntung kei Topa.
Ni khat, Amah pengkul in hong masuan ding,
Ama vanglian vantung pan hong tang ding;
Ka it ka ngaihte, Amah’n hong tonpih ding,
Angtan huai hi, tua Jesuh kei ading.
=== NGUN HILO, KHAM ZONG HILO ===
Key : D
Ngun hi lo, kham zong hilo, hong kitatkhiatna,
Leitung hauhnate in kei hong tan zo lo;
Kei muanna bulpi Jesuh si san bek hi a,
Ka Topa’ sihna in kei hong damsak zo.
Sakkik
Hong kitanzo, hih hang ngun hi kei,
Hong kilei zo, kham tawh hilo;
Jesuh sisan in keimah hong lei,
Hong itna genzawh hi lo.
Ngun hi lo, kham zong hilo, hong kitatkhiatna,
Ka lungsim mawhna vangik puakhin zo hi;
Kei muanna bulpi Jesuh si san bek hi a,
Ka Topa’ sihna bek in hong tan thei hi.
Ngun hi lo, kham zong hilo, hong kitatkhiatna,
Thukham in Pasian hong naihsak thei lo hi;
Kei muanna bulpi Jesuh si san bek hi a,
Ka Topa’ sihna in launa beisak hi.
Ngun hi lo, kham zong hilo, hong kitatkhiatna,
Vantung lampi lah kilei thei tuan lo hi;
Kei muanna bulpi Jesuh si san bek hi a,
Hong Honpa’ sihna bek in hong leizo hi.
=== NGAK NGIUNGEU ING ===
Key : G
Ngak ngiungeu ing, lungkia lo-in,
Meilum kaite a then dong;
Ngak ngiungeu ing, lungkia lo-in
Sun nitang lai a liap dong;
Ni khat a bang khang khat hun pan,
Lungkham khuamial ven mateng;
Nunna khuavak tang kiukiau-in,
Van aksite suah mateng.
An late in an sang khawmin,
sunkhum khit dong ka ngak hi;
Khua khal beiin hun kikhelta,
Phalbi huih dam nungta hi;
An late aw, khawm mengmeng un
Ka nuntak hun cing khinta;
Nuntakna pakpalh vul khinzo,
Ka nuntak hun beibei ta.
Vantung mite’n tua kep kongpi,
Ahon ding hun ka ngak hi;
Lung kia, thanem, zawngkhal kei mah’n,
Tua kongpi ah ka ngak hi;
Gamlapi ah, amau’ aw ging,
A kheging tu’n kiza ta;
Hong sap ding bek ke’n ka ngak hi,
A nungzui ding ka hita.
Ka muh ngeite sang a tangzaw,
Tenna’ng mun nuam ngak lah veng;
Nunna singkung pakzihziah a,
Niim dildial hi, mualkuam teng;
Ka Honpa in hong sangkik ding,
Tatna cing ngak ngiungeu ing;
Mawhna siat suah nuntakna le,
Dahna natna veng khin ding.
=== NGAI UN, VANTUNG MI’N LASA ===
Key : G
Ngai un! Vantung mi’n lasa,
A suak Topa minthan na;
Leitung nuamna hong khang sak,
Mawhna khempeuh phel ding ci,
Leitung mi khempeuh te in,
Lungdamna tawh tho un la;
Jesuh Bethlen ah suak hi;
Vanpi dong ah minthang hi
Vantungmite’n lasa hi,
“A suak Topa minthang” ci
Jesuh Topa Pasian Ta,
A om tawntung kumpi pa,
Nungak sung pan hong suak hi,
Mi bangin ah hong piang hi.
Pasian in mibang piang a,
Pasian itna mi sung ah;
Ka hong khawlkhawm sak nuam ci,
Emamuel Jesuh hi;
Vantungmite’n lasa hi,
“A suak Topa minthang” ci
Dawn un kilemna kumpi,
A thuman Ni bang tang hi;
Nuntak na leh khuavak na,
Hong puak suk khawm cidam na.
A vangliatna nusiat in, Eite sihloh na ding in;
Nihvei suak sak ding hong tuak,
Hong phongto dingin hong suak
Vantungmite’n lasa hi,
“A suak Topa minthang” ci
=== NGAI IN, KA KHA AW ===
Key : D
Ngai in, ka kha aw, vantung mi la sakna,
Leitung lungdam tuipi tung zong thang hi;
La pha sakna a aw zak nop huai bel hi,
Hing kikhel mawh kiphelna thu gen hi.
Sakkik
Thuciamna cing kham vantung mihingte in
A aw zaknop huai-in lasa uh hi;
Nitak kap a, zingsang ciang lungdamsak hi,
Sawtvei khuamial itna khuavak sak hi.
La aw zak ciang mailam nawtin i pai hi,
Lungkham a gimte aw hong pai un ci;
Khuamial sungah Topa Jesuh kiko hi,
Vantung inn lam hilhna thupha aw hi.
Gamlapi ah nitak siklong ging bangin,
Leitung, tui tung ah Jesuh’ aw ging hi;
Tul then tham lo, a vanlel mi tampite,
Tuucing Topa aw Na kiang hong pai hi.
Tu laitak i lungkham a sawt hang in-ah,
Khuamial kheng leng nuam na’ng khuavak ding hi;
A gimte zuihna lam a bei ciangin ah,
Kha Siangtho maang ding khamgam tung ding hi.

Hehpihna thupha midangte hawmsawn ding uh hi;
Topa’n a maute limtak kemin lungmuangsak dinga,
Amaute in vanah Pasian mai mu ding uh hi.

=== NA SIKKIP IN HONG LENZO DIAM? ===
Key : F
Na sikkip in hong lenkipzo na diam?
Huihpi hong nun ciang a muanhuai diam?

Hong lenkip zo diam? Na sikkip in.
Sakkik
Nuntakna hong len sikkip i nei,
Tuihual khan ciang zong launa’ng om kei
A kip suangpi tung khotak khih in,
Honpa itna sungah thukpi phum in.

Honpa’ khut in hong lung muangsak hi;
Ama lungtang pan, kei lungsim sungah,
Huihpi nan zawh na’ng hatna ka ngah.
Lauhuaina sungah hong lenkip ding hi,
Siat theihna hong nai i thei khol hi;
Huihsia hong nungin, tui kilok taleh,
Tuihual in hong tumzo ngei ke’n teh.
Hong lenkip ding hi, sihna tuihual sung,
Husan beidek dong huihsia hong nung;
Tuihual a hat hang i liing kei ding hi,
A kimulo lam-etna i nei.
Zan khuamial sung pan i gal-et ciangin,
Tembaw khawl mun tang kigalmuh khin;
Huihpi venna mun, vantung gun piau ah,
I sikkip khia ni, kiptak in-ah.

=== NA HOIHNA THUPHA KIGEN ===

=== NA DEIHNA BANG HITA HEN ===

Kamsiatna, dahna, kahna, thuak khata lecin,
Satan tawh kum tampi kidodo ta lecin,
Limtak thu zui-in lau ke’n, mainawt tawntung in.
“Lai Siangtho beel in ka nau aw.”
Na sim sialin thu thak khat thei khia den niteh,
Singtung a Jesuh’n hong sih lawhna thu hiveh;
Topa le vantung le nangma tung thuman veh,
“Lai Siangtho beel in ka nau aw.”
Tua laibu khuavak le upna sikkawipi hi,
Zan khuamial a, lam hong lak khuavak aksi hi;
Hong sawlna bang mang lecin, na maan den ding hi,
“Lai Siangtho beel in ka nau aw.”
=== LA THAK ===
Key : Bb
Jesuh mai-ah mi tampi kikhawm uh a,
A min phatna la sa in, gawsem tum uh hi.
Sakkik
Ei hong it a,
I mawhna hong phelsak Topa,
Ama min thang tawntung ta hen!
Amen, Amen.
Mawhna nei ngeite tua mihon maitang ah,
Puanpak silh in, sa uh hi,
Ama minphatna la.
A galte, siampi le kumpi suaksak hi,
A sipha tawh lei in, la thak a sa sak hi.
Hong tatkhiatna om kha zenzen lo hi leh,
Mawh nei mite bangzah in, i cimawh ding hiam.
Amah phatna aw nakpi in gingsak ni,
Midangte zong um a la thak a sak na’ng hi.
=== LA HONG SASA NUAM SAK DEN ===
Key : Ab
Ka lung sungah la ngaih hong kisa, Jesuh hong hopihna hi;
Lau ke’n nang kong ompih tawntung na,
Lungmaung takin om in, ci.
Sakkik
Jesuh, Jesuh, Jesuh,
Min teng pan ngaih pen;
Lunggulh teng kicinna,
La hong sasa nuamsak den.
Ka nuntakna mawhna’n su gawp zo, Lungsim sia, natna dimsak;
Jesuh’n asia teng hong lepsak zo,
A ngaih la khanglo kiksak.
Hong hehpihna pha tawh kivakin, A kha nuai ka beelzo ta;
A maitai ka muh tawntung manin,
Awngin la ka sa thei ta.
A sawt lo-in hong pai kik ding hi, Van ah hong la to dingin;
Theih loh gamah ka leeng to ding hi,
Amah tawh mangkhawm dingin.
=== KUMTHAK HONG TUNGTA ===
Key : Eb
Tu-in kum thak hong tung ta, Topa nong piaksa hi;
Sep ding bawl ding kum hi a, Nang tawh sep khop ding hi;
Mainawtna ding kum hi a, Kong phat ding kum a hi;
Nisim a nong ompihna, Theih telna ding kum hi.
Hehpihna kum thak hi a, Cihtak na’ng kum zong hi;
Na maipha muh kum hi a, Lung damna’ng kum thak hi,
Nong hehpihna ang-sung a, Kong ki ap kum a hi;
Lungnuam tawl dam hit-hiat a, Kong muan na’ng kumthak hi.
Nong itna thu gen khia a, Nasep na’ng kumthak hi;
Nasep siangtho sem ding a, Kipattah kum a hi;
Tu-in kum thak hong tung ta, Topa nong piaksa hi;
Leitung leh vantung teng a, Na minthan ding kum hi.
=== KUMPIPA TA KA HI ===
Key : F
Keima ka pa in na khempeuh nei hi,
Leitung sum khempeuh a khut sungah om hi,
Suang hoih, a san, a kang, kham, ngun a vekpi;
Kisim zolo-in Amah in a hau hi.
Sakkik
Kumpipa’ ta ka hi, Kumpi ta ka hi;
Hong Honpa Jesuh tawh Kumpipa ta ka hi.
Pasian tapa in mihing honkhia hi,
Mizawngte bangin leitungah a vak hi.
Tu-in vantung khua-ah a mang tawntung hi;
Nungciang vantungah omna hong pia ding hi.
Khatvei lai-inah khualmi bang ka hi,
Ka lunggulhna hangin mimawh ka suak hi.
Tu-in innluahna za, ka ngah na dingin;
Vantung khua suangah, keima min kigelh hi.
Puanbuk le lobuk a’ih hang phamawh kei,
Vantung ah innpi nuam ke’n nei khin ta ing.
Inn pan ka gamlat hang, ka lung a nuam hi;
Pasian min thang hen! Kumpipa’ ta ka hi.
=== KUMPIPA MAI I DING DING ===

Nung ciangin, nung ciangin.
=== KUMPIPA KONG BIANG HONG TUNG ZO ===
Key : G
Kumpipa kong biangah om hi,
Mawh neite’ tang sihna thuak Mi;
Mi siangthote bekmah tu-in,
Kaikhawm ding hong pai hi.
Sakkik
Kong biangah, kong biangah,
Kong biangah hi, kong biang tungzo;
Hong paita hi, hong paita hi,
Kong biang nangawn hong tungzo.
Hong pai ding nai na lak limte,
Kum simin kicing mengmeng hi;
Vantung zingsang khuavak tawntung,
Sawt lo i mu ding hi.
Kidona, gimna veng lo ding,
Leitung ah nopna zong kei in;
Honpa hong paikik ni ciangin,
Mawhna, sihna bei ding.
Van le lei thak i tun ciangin,
A tawntungin i teng ding hi;
Sihna om nawnlo nuntakna,
A tawntung hun zang ding.
=== KUMPIPA HONG MAKAI IN ===
Key : D
Kumpipa hong maikai in, uan ding ni hong tungzo;
Tu a kipan gal sungah, Nang buk ko inn hizo;
Kigin sung nong hehpihna’n, kote hong hatsak a;
Hing tawntung Kumpipa tawh, galdo la ka sa ta.
Kumpipa hong makai in mawhna gal bei mateng;
Gal kilemna nuam om a, sianthona’n zawh mateng;
Thau, tei le nam, khuangging tawh Pasian’ gam piang hi kei;
Ki-it kihehpihna tawh, Pasian gam hong tung thei.
Kumpipa’n hong makaih in, lau lo kong zui uh hi;
Na mai kimuhna peuh-ah, lungdamna khuavak hi;
Na singlamteh ko tungah, lam pai na’ng hong taan aw;
Galzawh lukhu’n hong ngak hi, Hong pi in Pasian aw.
=== KUMPIPA BIA UN ===
Key : A
Vang lian zahtak-huai Kumpipa bia un,
Lamdang hong itna, lungdamin sa un;
A hong liah, hong kem, hong uk tawntung Mangpa,
Vang-liatna tawh kidim phat huai Topa hi.
Nong kep nong huaina kigen zo lo-a,
Huih bang hong nung a, Khuavak bang tang ta,
Mualtung pan hong luang in, zang lei teng zel hi,
Daitui bang hong kia-in, guah bang hong zu hi.
Leivui tawh kibawl thanem mite in,
Nang kong muang uh hi, Nong huh den man in;
Nong hehpihna nuam in a tawntung kip hi,
Hong bawl, hong keem, hong tan, Lawmpha bel Na hi.
Kote Pa Pasian nong itna lian a,
Van-mite’n Nang mah hong phatna la sa;
Leitung mite in thanem mite hi ung,
Hih hang lungsim tak tawh Nang kong phat uh hi.
=== KUMPI LUKHU KHUSAK UN! ===
Key : Ab
Leitung mihingte aw en un, dahna thuak Jesuh ahi;
A gal khempeuhte zosak a, vantung mite phatsak hi
Sakkik
Kumpi lukhu, kumpi lukhu, Topa Jesuh khusak un!
Kumpi lukhu, kumpi lukhu, Topa Jesuh khusak un!
Vantung a misiang khempeuh in, Topa Jesuh min phat hi
Thukhen tokhom tung tusak a, vantung mite phatsak hi
Mi gilote’n ling tawh kigan, lukhu Jesuh khusak hi;
Mi siangtho le vantung mite’n, tu’n Jesuh a minphat hi
Ama min phatin kiko ni, gal zawh pawikhamna ngai un
Topa Jesuh in man ngah hi, lungdam huai bel hi, en un.
=== KUMPI LUKHU KHUSAK ===

Tu leh atawntungin.

Lukhu, Kumpi lukhu
Khusak in phat den ni.

Kumpite kumpipa.

=== KUM TAWN KHA TAWN HONG KEM TOPA ===
Key : G

Zingsang khuavak, Ni thak hong suak sial in,
Topa hehpihna bek kong ngak uh hi.
A beisa hun teng zong Na khut sung om, hong om-pih in.
Upna tawh thuciam na gam sung tun na’ng, Lam hong hilh in.
Khuamialna ah khuavak hong tang-sak in,
Upna lungsim khuavak hong nei sak in.
Mailam hun ding zong a thei khol Topa, kong zui uh hi.
Muanhuai mah le ung zong hong om pih in, Hong beel-beel nung.
Nuntak lai teng Nang, nuntakna khomun,
Ko hun bei ciang inn nuamah hong kha in.
=== KULHPI MUANHUAI I PASIAN ===
Key : C
Kulhpi muan huai Pasian hi a, sia theilo kidalna hi;
Tui khang bang gimna ah bia a, sihna ding pan hong hon hi,
Tang lai a i galpa’n i gimna ding zong saan;
Gilo in thahat-in, kihuatna hiam zangin,
Amah a gi lo pen hi.
Eima thatang bek i suan leh, i sepna mawkna suak ding;
Pasian teel pa’n hong huh kei leh, cikmahin i zo kei ding,
Na thei nuam hiam tua Pa? Jesuh Khris hi, tua Pa;
Mipi’ Topa Amin, kikhel lo tawntungin,
Amah’n gal A zo ding hi.
Siatna kidim hih leitung in, bawlsiat ding hong toto hi;
I thumanna gualzo dingin, Pasian in deih, leu kei ni,
Khuamial ukpa’ hawkna, kihta-in liing kei’n la;
A hehna thuak lai un, A lel hita, en un,
Kammal khat in zo ding hi.
Tua kammal pen khuamial ukte’ lungdamna ding hi lo hi;
Kha Siangtho le a thuphate, hong panpih Pa hong piak hi,
Neihsa lamsa bei thei, pumpi zong hong that thei;
Leitung nuntak bei thei, Pasian’ thu man kipin,
Ama’ gam kho den ding hi.
=== KUAN UN, PASIAN’ MITE ===

Ni bang ka tang den ding, Ni bang ka tang den ding.

‘Angaih mahmah late sa in,
Thangsak tawntung nuam ing Thangsak tawntung nuam ing’.
Lungnop ni hong tun tak ciang, Topa’n hong ciah pih ding a kiang;

Hong honpa Jesuh ka lawm tawh;

=== KONG PAI DING HI ===

=== KONG HONG KIU KIU KUA OM HIAM? ===

=== KITEEN NA LA ===
Key : Bb
Pasian in kiteenna pawi bawlkhinzo hi,
A siangtho innkuan a suak dingin;
A kicing innkuan khat a suah nadingin,
A siangtho nuntakna a nei ding.
Sakkik

I lawmte kiteenna pawi sungah;
Hih lungdamna thu vantung dong thangsak un,
Leitung nuntakna a bei ciangin.
Jesuh in Tapidawte a it manin,
A nuntakna a hong piak bangin;

=== KIKHOP NA LIAN ===
Key : C

Hotkhiatsate’ kikhopna lianpi hi ding!

Kikhopna lian! Kikhopna lian!

Kikhopna lian! Kikhopna lian!
Hotkhiatsate’ kikhopna lian vantung ah!
Ama sunga ihmusa mi Jesuh’n A thawhsak hun ciang,
A gamdai hankhuk le tuipi sung panin;
Siangtho pumpi nei-in vanah kilato ding Ama kiang,
Hotkhiatsate’ kikhopna lianpi hi ding!
“Omna tampi” a omna mun tua khuapi lian i et ciang,

Sihna in hong khensa lawmte nuamna tawh i muh hun ciang,
Hotkhiatsate’ kikhopna lianpi hi ding!

“Mit phiat kal sung hun tomno ah” eite i kikhel khin ding,
Hotkhiatsate’ kikhopna lianpi hi ding!
=== KI KHAWM DING INN PI AH ===
Key : Bb

Sakkik

A nuam gun pi le ciktui gei-ah;
Hong ngak i lawmte tawh,
Nuam in Topa min i phat ding hi.

I lawmte ei hong ngak in om ta;
Dahna tawh kipelh in i om ding hi,
Kimuh ciang lungdam in la sa ding.
Hong gum Topa Jesuh tokhom tung ah,
Lawmte aw a mai kikhawm in-ah;
Hong itna hong hehpihna a pha a,
A minthanna phat in la sa ni.

=== KHRISTIAN LIMTAK PAI ===
Key : G
Tapidaw limtak pai, launa hong nai,
Launa liinna sunga khual na zin lai;
A pua-ah thang, a sungah ze-etna,
Nungkiksak ding, hong zol mawhna sungah.
Tapidaw limtak pai, Tapidaw limtak pai,
Tapidaw limtak pai, launa hong nai.
Tapidaw nuam in pai, huihpi lak zong,
Kihtak huai vangingin khua a mial zong;
Huihpi le meiipi hong thengkik pah ding,
Tua ciang na Honpa tawh tawlnga den ding.
Tapidaw nuamin pai, Tapidaw nuamin pai,
Tapidaw nuamin pai, Huihpi lak zong.
Tapidaw ngen in pai, na pukkha ding,
Honpa na koh khialh leh na pukzel ding;
Thungetna galvante nang na silh leh,
Ze-etna haksa kantanzo niteh.
Tapidaw ngenin pai, Tapidaw ngenin pai,
Tapidaw ngenin pai, Na pukkha ding.
Tapidaw lam-en in nopna ngah ding,
Khawlmun tun ciang dahna natna bei ding;
“Na Topa tawh lungdam, nuamsa khawm in,”
Cihna za ding, Thukhenpa kam panin.
Tapidaw lam-en in, Tapidaw lam-en in,
Tapidaw lam-en in, Nopna ngah ding.
=== KHRISTIAN HOIH TE NUAM UN ===
Key : F
Tapidaw-te nuam un, lungdamin kipak un;
Kong thugen teng na ngai un,
Ngai un, tuni’n Jesuh hong suak hi;
Bawngte le late’n bia hi, tu-in gan an kuang sung om hi;
Khazih hong suak hi, Khazih hong suak hi.
Tapidaw-te nuam un, lungdamin kipak un;
Ngai un bei ngeilo nuamna,
Nuamna, nuam nading Jesuh suak hi;
Vantung kongpi hong zo hi, mihingte’n nuamsa den ding hi;
A hong suah manin, Ahong suah manin.
Tapidaw-te nuam un, lungdamin kipak un;
Sih ding tu-in lau nawnlo,
Lau lo, hong hon ding Jesuh suakzo;
Eite sap loh hong nei lo, Ama innpi sng kua ut lo;
Hong hon ding suakzo, hong hon ding suakzo.
=== KHRISTIAN “MANGPHA” ===
Key : Ab
It aw, nuam tak in ihmu in tawl nga in;

Hoih bel hi, kha ading, hoih bel hi.
Hong it a, anuam i ngaihsut ciang in-ah,
Ka mawh ka khialhna sung panin;
Ka suahtakna ding singlamteh tung si hi,
Ka lungsim in ka phat hi Topa.
Topa Jesuh tunung ciang hong pai ding hi,
Ka lungkhamna teng bei ding hi;
Topa hih leitung ah hong pai ding in-ah;
Ka Kha Siangtho ading apha hi.
Topa aw nong pai ding hun kong ngak uh hi,
Han hi lo, van hi, ko tupna;
Topa’ aw le van mite pengkul aw hi,
Ka lam-etna le ka tawl damna.
=== KA HUN NA KHUT SUNGAH ===
Key : Bb
Ka hun Na khut sungah, Topa kong ap khin hi;
Ka lawmte le ka pum ka kha, Topa kong ap khin hi.
Ka hun Na khut sungah, Nang deihna bang hihen;
Khuamial khuavak nopna dahna, Nang hoihsak bang hihen.
Ka hun Na khut sungah, patauh na’ng om ding hiam?
Ka pa’n a mawkna-in Ata, khitui a luangsak diam?
Ka hun Na khut sungah, kong ap tawntung ding hi;
Ka sih khit ciang na tak lamah, ka om tawntung ding hi.
=== KA HONPA’ HONG ITNA ===
Key : Ab
Nazareth mi Jesuh mai-ah lamdangsa-in ka ding hi;
Mawh nei niin bang kinawlkhin sa,
Ke nangawn a hong it hi.
Sakkik
Lamdang lua e! (Aw lamdang lua e!),
Pian dang lua e! (Aw pian dang lua e!)
Ka sak ding ka sak ding la; (Ka sak ding ka sak ding la)
Lamdang lua e (Aw lamdang lua e!),
Pian dang lua e! (Aw pian dang lua e!)
Ka Honpa’n kei hong itna (Ka Honpa’n kei hong itna).
Huan sungah thu hong ngetsak in,
“Nang deih bang hizaw hen” ci;
Ama adingin, luang lo-in
Kei hang khua-ul, si luang hi.
Van mite’n hehpih huaisa in,
Khuavak gam pan en uh hi;
Dahna hong thuaksak tua zanin,
Kei nem ding hong paisuk hi.
Ka mawh ka dahna teng la-in,
Ama tungah kisuan hi;
Kalvary ah tua van pua-in,
Amah bek in sihlawh hi.
Tatsate tawh minthang ding a,
Ama maitang ka mu ding;
Hong itna la ka sa dinga,
Khang tawngtung ka lungdam ding
=== KA HI BANGIN ===
Key : Eb
Ka hi bangin paulap nei lo,
Kei a’ ding na si luang simloh
Nangmah in Nong sapna thu tawh,
Pasian’ Tuuno’, kong zuan, kong zuan.
Ka hi bangin misia mittaw,
khuamuhna, hauhna, damna tawh;
Ka sapna teng ngah ding in aw,
Pasian’ tuuno, kong zuan, kong zuan.
Ka hi bangin mawhna baangin,
Kisil tawm dingin khawllo-in;
Na si’n hong siangsak thei manin,
Pasian’ Tuuno, kongzuan, kong zuan.
Ka hi bangin lungsim patau,
kisiatna tam, lungkiatna hau;
Sunglam, pualam, kaling kalau,
Pasian’ Tuuno, kong zuan, kong zuan.
Ka hi bangin nong sang mah ding,
Nongphel, nong sawp, nong huh mah ding;
Nang aa bek hi ta ning tu in,
Pasian’ Tuuno, kong zuan, kong zuan.
Ka hi bangin nong it manin,
Hong dal khempeuhte palsat in
Na thu ciamte ke’n umzo ing,
Pasian’ Tuuno, kong zuan, kong zuan
=== KA HI BANG HONG LA IN ===
Key : E
Topa Jesuh ka thungai in
Na hong phel kei leh ka si ding
Kiphel na thu hong pia suk in
Ka hi bang hong la in
Sakkik
Ka hi bang hong la in
Ka hi bang hong la in
Nang ma sih kei ma phatna hi
Ka hi bang hong la in
Phelna mu lo mawhna tampi
Ka neih manin Topa a si
Nong hehpih leh Nong phel thei hi
Bang mah a pha ka bawl zolo
Ka thu ciamna ka siasak zo
Na min tawh hong phel sak in aw
Ka hi bang hong la in
Na khe mai ah kong kun Topa
Nong muh bangin kei ka hi hi
Nasep kipan kiman khin zo
Ka hi bang hong la in
=== JORDAN GUN GEI AH ===
Key : G
Jordan gun gei ah ka dinga,
A gal lam ka en hi;
Kanaan gam nuam hong kilang a,
Ka luah nading gam hi.
Sakkik
Tua gam nuam sungah ei i khawl ding hi,
A nop tawntungna gungal khat-ah;
Nung ciangin Moses le Tuuno la sa ding hi,
Jesuh tawh mang tawntung ding hi.
Tua gam pha bel sungah inn-ah,
Khuavak tawntung om hi;
Pasian le Jesuh vang in-ah,
A tang tawntung ding hi.
Cikciang tua gam ka tung ding hiam,
Khuamial om lohna ah;
I Pa maitang lungdamna dim,
Cikciang ka mu ding hiam.
Ka sin sungah lungdam nading,
Leitung sawtpi om lo;
Jordan gunpi kilok hangin,
Lungdamin ka tum zo.
=== JESUH’N HONG IT HI ===
Key : Eb
Jesuh’n hong it ka thei hi
Lai Siangtho in hong gen hi
A neu a hat lo mite
A mah hat hong huh na ve
Sakkik
Jesuh’n hong it hi
Jesuh’n hong it hi
Jesuh’n hong it hi
Lai Siang-tho in gen hi
Jesuh’n hong it man si a
Van tung kong hong hon sak ta
Ka mawh na hong sawp sak ding
Van tung ah hong lut sak ding
Jesuh’n hong it manin ah,
Hong nai ka omna peuh a,
Amah it leng ka sih ciang,
Hong lato ding, Ama kiang.
=== JESUH SINGLAMTEH NUAI AH (A) ===
Key : Eb
Jesuh singlamteh nuai-ah, keimah ka khawl nuam hi;
Ni a sat phatna gam sungah, Suangpi liim bang ahi;
Gimna le tawlna gam sungah, Tawldamna innpi hi;
Vangik puate’n van khia dinga, A gimte’ khawlna’ng hi.
Jesuh singlamteh liim ah, khawlmun nuam pen ahi;
Vantung itna le thu manna, kituahna mun ahi;
Mi siangthote’n a mang sungah, Amuh kahlei bang hi;
Tua sing khuam kei ading hi-a, vantung kahlei ahi.
Singlamteh galmuh khop ah, Nilim liap khat om hi;
A lipkhap huai hankhuk hi-a, zai-in thuk mahmah hi;
Tua hankhuk le ei kikalah singlamteh khat om hi;
Singlamteh in lam hong laka, van gam lam hong hilh hi.
Jesuh’n singlamteh tungah, kei tang gimna thuak hi;
A thuak gimna ka ngaihsun a, hong itna ka mu hi;
Khitui luang kawm ka lungsim ah, thu nih ka phawk thei hi;
Ka mawhna le a hong itna, hih thute gel ahi.
Jesuh’n singlamteh liim mah, keima omna ahi;
Amai vangtang longal van-ah, Nitang kisam lo hi;
Leitung nopsakna le hauhna, ka lunggulh nawn kei hi;
Ka mawhnate zumna hi-a, singlamteh meetna hi.
=== JESUH OM NA DING MUN NA NEI HIAM ===
Key : C
Na mawhna tang a thuak Jesuh,
Omna ding mun a om hiam?
Kong khak kiu-in lut ding hong tu,
Mawh neite’n a ngai na diam?
Sakkik
Topa Jesuh minthang Kumpi!
A omna’ng mun tu’n bawl ini!
Na lungsim kongkhak tanzau in!
Hong in na lutsak ding hi!
Na lung sunggah na omsak leh,
Nuamna hong bawlsak ding hi;
Omna’ng na omsak loh hangin,
Na mawhna tang ding si hi.
Topa Ejsuh in a hun ciang,
A thupha tawh hong sam ding;
Tuni’n a thupha sang inla,
Zing iang ngak kei leteh pha.
Omna’ng mun le hun na pia in,
A nuam ding ni khengsak ke’n;
Sawt lo-in hong sam pakkha leh,
Na lungsim khauhsak kei in.
=== JESUH’ MIN MANPHA NA LA IN ===
Key : Ab
Jesuh’ min manpha na la in
Dahna’ gimna’ tate aw
Hehnep nuamna hong pia ding in
Na paina peuhah keng aw
Sakkik
Min manpha, ngaih mahmah
Leitung mite’ lam-etna
Min manpha ngaih mahmah
Vantungah lungdam nuamna.
Jesuh’ min na kem tawntung in
Gal namkim kidalna lum
Ze-etna’n hong kimkot ciangin
Amin siangtho suangin thum
Jesuh’ min a manpha mahmah
Bangzah i lung hong damsak
Hong saan’ ciang A ma angsung ah
A ma la i sak laitak
Lam tawp vantung i tun’ ciangin
Jesuh’ khe ah i bok ding
Kumpi khempeuh tung Kumpi ci’n
Ama mai-ah i bia ding
=== JESUH MIN ===
Key : C
Jesuh min bang zahin ngaih hiam,
Ama’ late sasa nuam ing;
Ka lung hong kimsak mahmah hi,
Jesuh A man manpha hi.
Sakkik
‘Jesuh’ bangzah a ngaih min,
‘Jesuh’ Nisimin tuamah;
‘Jesuh’ kici min manpha, phat tek ni,
A tawntung in.
Ka lungsim le ka dahna teng,
A theikhin pa’ min ngaih ka sa;
Launa lungmannate beisak,
Jesuh Amin ka it hi.
Tua min ngaih ka zaza nuam hi,
Ka lungsim hong nopsak khial kei;
Ama late’n khitui nulsak,
Jesuh Amin thangsak un!
Kuamah’n gen thei ngei het lo hi,
Tua ka it min, bangzah’n ngaih hiam;
Aw tua min phatna bek ging hi,
Jesuh A min phat ve un.
=== KHRIS GALKAPTE’N AH ===
Key : F
Khazih galkapte’n ah, galsim ding kuan un;
Eite mai a masa, Jesuh mitsuan un;
Khazih eite Mangpa, makai hilo maw;
En un a dialpaina, galphual lam manawh!
Sakkik
Jesuh’ galkapte’n ah, galkap ding kuan un;
Singlamteh pua un la, Na mailam nawt un.
Jesuh min a zak ciang, dawi mite tai uh;
Nawt un, tua ahih ciang, Na mualsuah dong uh;
Phatna aw kizak ciang, dawi gam kiliing hi;
Lawmte tua ahih ciang, awng un phatna pi.
Galkap honpi bangin, Pawlpi’n masot hi;
Tang mi siangte bangin, I totna khat hi;
Eite kikhen lo-in, pum khat bek i hi;
Lawp le zuih kikhat-in, hong ki-itsak hi.
Kumpi za sia thei hi, Kumpi gam kip kei;
Hih hang Jesuh Pawlpi, cikmah’n sia thei kei;
Dawi in Pasian’ Pawlpi, Cikmah’n zo ngei kei;
Khazih hong ciamsa hi, A ciampeel ngei kei.
Tua hi a hong pawm un, mi khempeuh in-ah;
Ko tawh hong sa khawm un, galzawh nuamna la;
A minthang pahtawi un, leitung vantung ah;
Tatsat lo-in phat un, Khazih Kumpipa.
=== JESUH A GALKAPTE MAKAIH ===
Key : C
Ngai un, sapna aw in, tuni’n kua kuan ding;
Ka thu hong nial loin, kua’n ka nasem ding?
Kua’n ka dialkhai tawi ding, kua’n galdo ding hiam?
Thuman Pasian ading, kua teng kuan ding hiam?
Sakkik
Jesuh’n dialkhai nuai-ah, galdo makaih hi;
Hih leitung gal khempeuh, thuman tawh zo hi.
Pasian’ hotna muang in, gal i zawh mateng;
Satan zawh nadingin, galvan hoihte keng;
A siangtho tupna ah, thumanin ding ni;
Pasian’ adingin ah, khut le khe zang ni.
Galkap honpite in, pai kawmin lasa;
Phat ni Kumpipa min, eite makaipa;
I tup lian kibang hi, a nai a gamla,
I awging kiza hi, kuanin mainawt un.
=== JESUH, NANG KONG NGAIHSUT CIANG ===
Key : A
Jesuh thu ngaihsut laitakin,
Lungdam huai mahmah hi;
Hih sang a mai ka muh ciangin,
Lungdam zaw lai ding hi.
Jesuh a kici min sangin,
Min ngaih zaw om lopi;
Vantung leitung ahi zongin,
Kimu zo ngei lo hi.
Dahna thuakte’ kihehnepna,
Lung niamkhiatte nuamna;
Thungen a zong mite ading,
Itna lian bel hita.
Kam tawh a kigenkhia theilo,
Thupha a ngah uh hi;
A kisim khin zolo itna,
Topa Jesuh thu hi.
Topa Jesuh nangmah simloh,
Nuamna dang om nawn lo;
Tu le nung iang a tawntungin,
Komau phat ding om in.
=== JESUH VA KO NING ===
Key : Eb
Jesuh va ko ning, ka haksatna teng,
Kei kia’n pua zo ke’ng ka van lompi;
Hong puak pih ding hi, Amah va suan leng,
Kei hong it in hong kem tawntung hi.
Sakkik
Jesuh va ko ning! Jesuh va ko ning!
Kei kia’n pua zo ke’ng, ka van lompi;
Jesuh va ko ning! Jesuh va ko ning!
Kei a hong huh thei Jesuh bek hi.
Jesuh va ko ning ka lungkhamna teng,
Hong hehpih thei pen ka lawmpa hi;
Hong huhpah ding hi, va ko manpeuh leng,
Ka lung gimna teng veng pah ding hi.
Ze-et bawlsiatna, ke’n thuakkha zel ing,
Hong honpa lo in ka om thei kei;
Jesuh va ko ning, Jesuh va ko ning,
Amah bekbek hi, kei hong hon thei.
Leitung in hong zol ka siat-theih na ding,
Ka lungsim sung ah siatna dim hi;
Bangbang ka tuak zong Jesuh va ko ning,
Amah’n leitung hong zawhpih ding hi.
=== JESUH THU THEI SEMSEM NUAM INGH ===
Key : Ab
Jesuh thu thei semsem nuam ingh.
Hong itna thu gengen nuam ingh.
Kei tang a si Pa hong itna,
A cing zaw in ka thei nuamta.
Sakkik
A thu zaza nuam ing
A thu zaza nuam ing
Kei tang a si Pa hong itna
A cing zaw in ka thei nuam ta.
Jesuh thu ken sinsin nuam ingh.
A deihna khen tel thei nuam ingh.
Pasian Kha Siangtho ka sia pa’n
Khris zia le tong hong lak khia ta’n
Jesuh kammal zaza nuam ingh.
Topa tawh holim den nuam ingh.
A aw ngai ning vai khempeuh ah,
A gen teng ka pom nuam ta.
Van tokhom ah a tutna thu,
Van hauhna teng a neihna thu;
A gam zai na’ng leh hong pai na’ng
Za nuam ing, Kumpi a suah na’ng.
=== JESUH TAWH TON PEUH LENG ===
Key : C
Launa namkim omna mualkuam thuk sung ahi zong,
Lungnuam a ka omna ni tang khuavak sung hizong;
Khuasia khuapha taleh, thuhoih khat ken thei ing,
Jesuh tawh ton peuh leng, koima peuh pai ning.
Sakkik
Jesuh tawh ton leng mun khempeuh ka pai ding,
Ama omna peuh vantung hipah ding, kei ka om ding;
A singlamteh ke’n ka pua ding, ka hampha ding
Jesuh tawh ton leng, mun khempeuh ka pai ding.
Sehnel nisa kanin mawhna, gal le sa lakah,
Nuntak thupha puakin ka pai ding phamawh hi-a;
Ka mel bangbang pua-in tua munah ka pai ding,
Jesuh tawh ton peuh leng koima peuh pai ning.
Midangte’n tuipi gal kanin a sep laitakin,
Kei puak ding singlamteh tual sung teng ahi zongin;
A thupiakna mangin upna kipin om ning,
Kei hong ompihna koi ma peuhah om ning.
Ka Topa’ thupiakna ke’n ka nial ding hilo hi,
Hong hilhna kammalte ke’n ka zuih ding hizaw hi;
Inn ah omzaw ding maw khual gamla paizaw ding,
Honpa tawh hi peuh leng koi peuh lungkim ing.
=== JESUH TAWH MUN KHEMPEUH AH (B) ===
Key : D
Jesuh tawh mun khempeuh ka pai khawm ding hi
Kikhen lo in hong khakna ka zui ding hi
A khe kiangah tu leh launa om lo a,
Jesuh tawh mun khempeuh ka pai khawm ding hi
Sakkik
Pai khawm, Jesuh tawh paikhawm ding,
Pai khawm mun khempeuh pai ding;
Pai khawm, Jesuh tawh paikhawm ding,
Mun khempeuh ah Jesuh tawh pai ding.
Mun khempeuh kei guak hi keng Jesuh tawh hing,
Lawmte’n nusia hangin, Jesuh kei aa hi;
Lam haksa hang a khut tawh hong kha ding a,
Jesuh tawh mun khempeuh ka pai khawm ding hi.
Jesuh tawh mun khempeuh kei ka lum thei a,
Sihna a liim in hong kimkot hang in ah
Ka thawh ciang kawivak nawn lo ding ka thei hi
Jesuh tawh mun khempeuh ka pai khawm ding hi.
=== JESUH TAWH MUN KHEMPEUH AH (A) ===
Key : D
Jesuh tawh mun khempeuh ka pai khawm ding hi,
Kikhen lo in hong khakna ka zui ding hi;
A khe kiangah tu leh launa om lo a,
Jesuh tawh mun khempeuh ka pai khawm ding hi
Sakkik
Pai khawm ding, mun khempeuh
launa om thei kei
Jesuh tawh mun khempeuh ka pai khawm ding hi
Mun khempeuh kei guak hi keng Jesuh tawh hing,
Lawmte’n nusia hangin, Jesuh kei aa hi;
Lam haksa hang a khut tawh hong kha ding a,
Jesuh tawh mun khempeuh ka pai khawm ding hi
Jesuh tawh mun khempeuh kei ka lum thei a,
Sihna a liim in hong kimkot hang in ah
Ka thawh ciang kawivak nawn lo ding ka thei hi
Jesuh tawh mun khempeuh ka pai khawm ding hi.
=== JESUH TANGTHU KEI HONG GEN IN ===
Key : Eb
Jesuh tangthu kei hong hilh in,
A thu ka lung sung gelh in;
A manpha tangthu hong gen in,
Zak ngei nai loh thukhum pen.
A suah lai vantung mite sak, la n gaihte hong sak dih in;
Sang belna ah Pasian thang hen,
Leitung kilemna om hen.
Sakkik
Jesuh tangthu kei hong hilh in,
Athu ka lung sung gelh in;
A manpha pen Jesuh tangthu,
Kei hong ciamteh thei sak in.
Sehnel gam an ngawnl in om a,
Ahih teng hong gengen in;
Ei mawhna hang ze-etna thuak,
Thuak hang a zawh teiteina.
A thuak kum sung hong gen dih in,
Dahna gimna a puak teng;
Bawlsiat, cilphih a thuakna teng,
Simmawh nilkhiat a thuakna.
Singlamteh ah kilh a thuakna,
Na sa’n lunggim a omna;
Han sung guanga, a kicinna,
Sihna pan a hinkikna.
=== JESUH TANGTHU HONG GEN DIH IN ===
Key : C
Jesuh tangthu hong gen dih in, ke’n za nuam ing;
Hih lai-ah hong om hileh, bang ka gen ding hiam,
Lam gei a muh teng, tuipi tangthu,
Jesuh’ tangthute kei hong hilh in.
Naupangte tawh a kikholhna, ke’n mu nuam ing;
Tua ciang, Ama thuphate ke’n zong ngah nuam ing,
Gitna kam bek dim hehpihna dim,
Itna khuavak taang Jesuh maitang.
Khuapi sungah ka zui ding hi, naupang hon tawh;
Dial lekin, nisuh hiang tawi-in khut tawh lamin,
“Hosanna” ci-in Jesuh Kumpi!
Amah phatna la nakpi’n sa ning.
=== JESUH SUNGAH KIKHEN LO HI ===
Key : Eb
Jesuh sungah kikhen lo hi, Ni suah, ni tum sak, khang;
Leitung khempeh kua mi, kua mi, lawm khat pawl khat hi hang.
Jesuh sungah lungsiim mante’n, pawl ngah kawikawi ding hi;
Ama nasepna, miteng henkhawm, kham khau zang bang hi.
Khut kilen ni up kikhat teng, u le nau bang hihang;
Bang nam hi leng, Pa’ nasem teng, beh khat phung khat hihang.
Jesuh sungah, i kimat hi, sakmi, khang mi, paam mi;
Jesuh lungsim banga nei, mi khempeuh pumkhat suak hi.
=== JESUH SAPNA AW NGAI UN ===
Key : Db
Ngai un! Jesuh’ hong sapna aw, “Tuni kua in nasem ding?
Lote au khin anlak hunzo, Tangte kua in kaikhawm ding?”
Topa’n tu’n zong hong sam lai hi, Thaman tampi hong lui hi;
Kua in dawng ding lungdam takin: “Topa aw, kei hong sawl in.”
Tuipi galna kai zawh loh hang, Lawki gam na pai lah zong;
Na kong biang ah na huh theih dang, Na kiang nai zong om theizaw;
Van mi bang na pau thei kei zong, Jesuh’ hong itna gen aw;
Paul bang thu na hilh thei kei zong, Topa hong si hi, ci aw.
Zion kulhpi sang tung panin, Galvilna hi zolo zong;
Na hilh thei lo zong van lami, nuntakna na lui lah zong;
Thungetna le sumpite tawh, vantung deihna sem thei ding;
Kamsangpa’ khutte a domto, Aaron bang na hi thei ding.
Mihingte a sih laitakin, Topa’n nang hong samlai hi;
“Bangmah ka sem thei kei” ci-in, Thadah kampau khia kei in;
Hong sawl peuh lungdam tak sem in, Thu nuamtakin semta in;
Dawng pah in, a hong sap cinagin “Topa aw, kei hong sawl in.”
=== JESUH NANGMA DEIH BANG ===
Key : Eb
Jesuh, Nangma deih bang, Keimah’n zong deih nuam ing;
Nangma itna khut sung, hong ki-ap khin nuam ing.
Dahna nuamna sungah, Nangmah’n hong tonpih in;
Cizo nuam ing, Topa “Nang deih bang hisak in.”
Jesuh, Nangma deih bang, luankhi’n liah zel zongin;
Ka upna aksi tang, mualsak, mangsak kei in.
Nang zong hih leitungah, na dah na kah manin;
Nang tawh kap dingin-ah, “Nang deih bang hisak in.”
Jesuh, Nangma deih bang, kei ading pha khin hi;
Mailam a piang bangbang, Nangmah kong apkhin hi.
Lung patau lo keimah, Tangtak ka zuan van inn;
Hin lai, sih ciang, ka la, Nang deih bang hisak in.”
=== JESUH MUANG IN ===
Key : Ab
Nisimin Jesuh a min, umin huihpi nun ciangin;
Thu upna tawm hangin, Jesuh bek umin muang in.
Sakkik
Nisimin Jesuh Topa, umin beel in muang inla;
Lai Siangtho hong hilh bangin, Jesuh bek umin muang in.
Kha Siangtho keima tungah, hong taang hi, ka sin sungah;
Lam hong hilh leh puk zolo, Jesuh bek umin muang in.
Lam a nop leh la sa ta, khua hong mial le thuum inla;
Gimna thuak ciang thungen in, Jesuh bek umin muang in.
Ka nuntak lai teng muang ning, leitung bei mateng suang ning.
Vantung khua tun mateng in, Jesuh bek umin muang in.
=== JESUH KUMPI SUAK HI ===
Key : Eb
Jesuh Kumpi suak a, van tokhom tung tu hi;
Kumpi lukhu kikhusak a, mi siangte’n pahtawi hi.
Sakkik
Tat (khiat) sa mi siangte tawh,
Lung (sim) muangin Honpa tawh,
I lung a kim ding hi, Nung (nung) ciangin!
Nung ciangin! Nung ciang!
I lung a kim ding hi, nung ciangin!
Sim zawh loh mi honpi’n, puanpaak silh tee zihziah;
Pahtawina nisuh hiang tawi-in, phatna la sa ziahziah.
Amau ading sipa, Tuuno a phat uh hi;
Tuuno’ sisan hang kilemna, lukhu khu ciat uh hi.
Kha Siangtho hehpihna, Ko ading nong pia hi;
Gualzo mi siangte tawh van-ah, Nong kipawl khawmsak hi.
=== JESUH KIANGAH KA PIA DING HI ===
Key : D
Hong gum Topa kei mah in ah
Na khempeuh paai in zui ning
Ka Topa aw Nang mah in ah
Lam honghilh Pa Na hi ding
Sakkik
Na khempeuh paai a, Na khempeuh paai a
Na khempeuh Topa khut sungah
Kei mah’n hong pai ning
Hong gum Topa kei mah in ah
Nang ma kiang ka hong nai hi
Ki sik a thu pha kong ngetna
Ngai in hong gum in kong ci,
Hong gum Topa kei mah in ah
Leitung nopna ka nusia
Kha Siangtho le Topa Pasian
Hong om in ka lungsungah
=== JESUH KIANG NA PAI HIAM? ===
Key : Ab
A siangtho ngah ding Jesuh kiang na pai diam?
Tuuno si tawh na ki sawp zo hiam?
A thupha kicing ding in na um nai hiam?
Tuuno si tawh na ki sawp zo hiam?
Sakkik
Tuuno a (Tuuno a) sipha tawh (sipha tawh)
Nangmah in na kisawp siang zo maw? (siang zo maw?)
Na puansilh vuk bang in-ah na ngah zo hiam?
Tuuno si tawh na ki sawp zo hiam?.
Nisim in Topa kiangah lam na zui hiam?
Tuuno si tawh na kisawp zo hiam?
Thahna a thuak Topa kiang na beel ta hiam?
Tuuno si tawh na ki sawp zo hiam?
Mopipa hong pai ciang na puan siang dingin,
Tuuno si tawh na kisawp zo hiam?
A bawl innpi nuam ah lut theih na dingin,
Tuuno si tawh na kisawp zo hiam?
Mawhna khialhna a baang na puansilh pai in,
Tuuno si tawh na kisawpzo hiam?
A siang lo na lungsung ciktui luang sak in,
Tuuno si tawh na ki sawp zo hiam?
=== JESUH KIA’N SINGLAMTEH PUA ===
Key : A
Jesuh kia’n singlamteh pua a
Guak pai ding maw lei mi
Hi lo, mikim puak ding om a
Kei puak ding zong om hi
Singlamteh ke’n ka pua ding hi
Sihna’n hong khah ma teng
Kumpi lukhu ka ngah ding hi
Vantung innpi tung leng
A kikhen let Jesuh khe kiang
Lim lang suang phah tung ah
Ka kham lukhu ka ngak suk ciang
Nuam in phat ning Amah
Aw manpha hi, tua singlamteh
Vaanglian kumpi lukhu
Ka ngah ding hi hinkikna leh
Hong lak ding lawpna thu
=== JESUH KHRIH HONG HONPA ===
Key : G
Van pan hong kumsuk kua hiam?
Jesuh Khris hong Honpa!
Kiniamkhiat a suak kua hiam?
Jesuh Khris hong Honpa!
Sakkik
Sa un, Ama min phatna,
Hotkhiatna hong tunzo ta;
Eite hong it penpen pa,
Jesuh Khris hong Honpa!
Singkhuam tung kikhai kua hiam?
Jesuh Khris hong Honpa!
Nang le kei hong tan kua hiam?
Jesuh Khris hong Honpa!
Mawhmai na’ng kua’n hong ciam hiam?
Jesuh Khris hong Honpa!
Um in hing un, kua’n ci hiam?
Jesuh Khris hong Honpa!
Van tokhom tung kua tu hiam?
Jesuh Khris hong Honpa!
I it i zuih ding kua hiam?
Jesuh Khris hong Honpa!
Van pan kua hong kumkik diam?
Jesuh Khris hong Honpa!
A mite khawm ding kua hiam?
Jesuh Khris hong Honpa!
=== JESUH KHEPHUNG AH KA TU HI ===
Key : F
Jesuh khe phungah ka tu-a,
Hong hopihna ka za hi;
Itna kam khum bekbek hi a,
Nisim ka zaza nuam hi;
Jesuh khephung ah ka tu a,
Tang lai thute ka phawk hi;
Hong it pha mahmah na hi a,
Ka lungsim sung hong zen hi.
Jesuh khephung ah ka tawlnga a,
A nuamzaw mun omlopi;
Ka vangik pi teng ka suahna,
Ka tawldamna mun ahi;
Jesuh khephungah ka tawlnga,
Ka deih khempeuh ka ngen hi;
Ka nget khempeuh A hong pia a,
Hong piak loh om ngeilo hi.
Hong Hon Topa Na thupha tawh,
Tu-in keimah hong hh in;
Hong en in, Na itna mit tawh,
Na maipha hong musak in;
Nangma lungsim kei hong guan aw,
Na sian bang hong siangsak in;
Midik hong tansak Jesuh aw,
Gen ing, kei Nang aa hi khin.
=== JESUH KEI AA DING HI ===
Key : D
Topa Pasian lo ngal vanah
Muan ding dang om lo hi
Nuntak lai teng ka sak ding la,
Jesuh kei aa ding hi
Topa’n kei tang gimna thuak hi
A sipha tawh hong sawp zo hi
Lungsim siang tho hong guan’zohi
Jesuh kei aa ding hi.
Mi a haute ka eng kei hi
Jesuh kei aa ding hi
Leitung sum ke’n ka deih kei hi
Jesuh kei aa ding hi.
Leitung hauhna kip lo ding hi
Na khempeuh kisia gawp ding hi
Kei nuamna bei thei lo ding hi
Jesuh kei aa ding hi
Zawng a gimna ka thuak hangin
Jesuh kei aa ding hi
Ka thum nop loh Topa’n thei hi
Jesuh kei aa ding hi
Ka sum khempeuh ka zang zong in
Leitung sum a sia khin zong in
Ganhing teng a si khin zong in
Jesuh kei aa ding hi.
Galte khut sung ka tung zongin
Jesuh kei aa ding hi
Kisiatna in hong um hangin
Jesuh kei aa ding hi
Leitung gal a kido hang in
Ka kha in a kap hang in ah
Topa min tawh ka zo ding hi
Jesuh kei aa ding hi.
=== JESUH KA LUNGSIM IN KA DEIH ===
Key : C
Jesuh ka lungsim in ka deih
Hong heh pih na nak pi’n ka ngen
Hong heh pih na it nahong lang
Amah ke’n ka it pha sem ta
Sakkik
Lungsim phabel hong guan suk in
Tua Kham khuapi ka muh nading
Ka lungsim sung hong taang sak in
Tua khua pi nuam kei a ding hi
Lei tung itna sung a nuampen
Ki teh thei lo Hong it na tawh
Kong en to lam et na pi tawh
Na mai muh ciang lamdang ka sa
Van tung gam sung nop na kidim
Paak te hoih na mu ding tua lai
Za nawn lo ding vantung mi aw
Ka kha in lam dang sa ding ta
Nang loin nopna om thei kei
Ka lungsim hong dam sak thei ding
Nang Na om ciang dahna nuam sak
Vantung nopna kei sung hong taang
=== JESUH KA LUNG SUNG AH HONG LUT PHET IN ===
Key : A
Topa Jesuh ka lung sungah hong lut phet-in,
Ka lungsim hong kikhel pah hi!
Topa Jesuh ka lung sungah hong lut phet-in,
Ka lung sung khua hong vak pah hi!
Sakkik
Topa Jesuh ka lung sungah,
Hong tum hong khawl khit phet in-ah;
Tuipi kilok bang ka lung sungah khuavakna,
Thakhat-in a hong tang pah hi.
Topa Jesuh ka lung sungah hong lut phet-in,
Lam ka khial nawn kei pah ding hi!
Topa Jesuh ka lung sungah hong lut phet-in,
Ka mawh khempeuh hong sawp siang hi!
Topa Jesuh ka lung sungah hong lut phet-in,
Upna a kip ka ngah pah hi!
Topa Jesuh ka lung sungah hong lut phet-in,
Up khialhna teng bei khin pah hi!
Topa Jesuh ka lung sungah hong lut phet-in,
Sihna kuam sung khuavak pah hi!
Topa Jesuh ka lung sungah hong lut phet-in,
Khuapi kong khak kimu pah hi!
=== JESUH IN TANG DINGIN HONG SAWL ===
Key : G
Jesuh in eite khuaimei vak bangin,
Zan khuamialna sungah tangin hong sawl hi;
Hih leitung khuamial sungah i tang ding,
Nang na omna kiim ah, kei, kei’ kiim ah.
Jesuh’n hong tangsak Ama adingin,
I meivak a mial ciang Amah’n hong mu hi;
I meivak tang van pan Amah’n ensuk,
Nang na omna kiim ah, kei, kei’ kiim ah.
Jesuh’n hong tangsak miteng adingin,
Khuamialna tampi tawh kidim hih leitung;
Mawhna, dahna, natna sung i tang ding,
Nang na omna kiim ah, kei, kei’ kiim ah.
=== JESUH IN NANGMA DAHNA A THEI HI ===
Key : Ab
Dahna a om khempeuh, Topa Jesuh’n thei;
Lungsim kisikna le thungetna zong thei;
Lau keei lo-n um in, na lungkhauhsak in;
Na van Topa suan in, hong nuamsak ding hi.
Ama lungsim sungah, Nang pha hong sa hi;
Na galte khut sung pan, Nang hong gum ding hi;
Ama deihna bangin, lam hong hilh ding hi;
A vaang tanna lamah na tung thei ding hi.
Gal na do Jesuh’n thei, Na thuumna za hi;
Na lunggim lam zong thei, na kiko za hi;
Na kha tha khauhna’ngin, na tai loh na’ngin;
Lungsim nuam hong pia ding na khitui nul ding.
=== JESUH IN HONG SAM ===
Key : C
Jesuh in itna tawh inn ah hong sam;
Tuni’n hong sam, tuni’n hong sam;
Ni bang tang hong itna pan a pualam,
Bang ding kidai thah na hiam?
Sakkik
Tuni’n hong sam, Tuni’n hong sam;
Jesuh in hong sam,
Hong it manin tuni’n hong sam.
Jesuh’n hong pia nuam a gimte tawldam;
Tuni’n hong sam, tuni’n hong sam;
Na van va puak inla, ngah in lungdam,
Nang a hong nial kei ding hi.
Jesuh’n hong ngak hi, pai in tu laitak;
Tuni’n hong ngak, tuni’n hong ngak;
Na mawhna mah tawh va kun in niamtak,
Pai in kizekai sak ke’n.
Jesuh in hong zol hi, A aw ngai in:
Tuni’n za in, tuni’n za in,
Nuamna ngah ding hi, Amah umte in,
Tho in paipah vingveng in.
=== JESUH IN HONG KEM HIAM ===
Key : Db
Ka lampi sau-in a gim huai-a,
Vangik pua-in kikem khialin;
Ka lampi sau-in, lungsim a nat ciangin,
Jesuh in kei a hong kem hiam?
Sakkik
A hong kem hi, ke’n ka thei hi,
Ka dahna hong thuakpih hi,
Sunin om nuam lo-in, zana lauhuai laitak
Hong gumpa’n hong kem.
Sun khuavak in a hong mial ciangin,
Kei kiangah a hong nai om hiam?
Ka lampi mialin, lauhuai a tam ciang,
Jesuh in kei a hong kem hiam?
Haksa ze-et ka thuak laitakin,
Zan tawntung khitui luanna tawh;
Hong hon ding omlo ka dah laitakin,
Jesuh in kei a hong kem hiam?
I itte tawh mangpha kipia-in,
Lungkham lutang nat a bei ciang;
Topa in ei bang ci-in hong mu diam,
Jesuh in kei a hong kem hiam?
=== JESUH IN HONG GUM HI ===
Key : G
Lungdamna thupha ka za, “Jesuh in hong gum hi!”
Tua thupha na gen inla, “Jesuh in hong gum hi!”
Gam khempeuh ah pai inla, Mual kal, gungal kan dinga;
Va gen in Topa thupha, “Jesuh in hong gum hi!”
Gunpi kan in kiko in, “Jesuh in hong gum hi!”
Gamla nai mi kiang gen in, “Jesuh in hong gum hi!”
Tuikulh panin kiko in, A gal-khat na thawn sak in;
Leitungah lungdamna in, “Jesuh in hong gum hi!”
Gal kapna sung kiko in, “Jesuh in hong gum hi!”
Singlamteh tung sihna in, “Jesuh in hong gum hi!”
Hehpihna i deih ciangin, Tua thute na ngaihsun in;
Sihna zawh man lasa in, “Jesuh in hong gum hi!”
Leitungah na kiko in, “Jesuh in hong gum hi!”
Mi khempeuh lungdamsak in, “Jesuh in hong gum hi!”
Mual tung le kuam thuk sungah, Hong phelna thu gen in-la;
Hih zawhna thu lasakna, “Jesuh in hong gum hi!”
=== JESUH HONG TUN MA TENG ===
Key : F
Gimna sung pan lam-et gam nuam
cik ciang ka tung ding hiam?
Cik ciang gal van ka koih ding hiam?
Lai lung ka muang ding hiam?
Sakkik
Jesuh hong tun ma teng,
Jesuh hong tun ma teng,
I na sep zawh ciangin
Inn nuam sung om khawm ding
Sim leitung lai lungdam om lo
Lum bang sung om lo tawh
Sim leitung sau nuam a hi lo
Gam bang daihna ahi.
Lim bel siangtho ngah ding in ah
Lam bang na pial ke’n ci leng
Van siang nuam ka tun ma teng
Nuamna ong pia ding hi
Lim bel nen ah khawl zo ta in
Lam sawn ka pial kei ding
A mah bang a ka pham nung ciang
Leng van siang nuam tung ning
=== JESUH HONG PAI DING HI ===
Key : Bb
La sa un! “Jesuh in kong pai ding” ci,
A si tawh a gup mihing ta dingin;
Hong kum a, hong uk ding a minthang hi,
Jesuh hong paikik ding hi!
Sakkik
Jesuh hong pai ding, hong paikik ding hi,
Jesuh hong paikik ding hi!
Lungdamin, la pha sa un nuam ding hi!
Jesuh hong paikik ding hi!
Jesuh hong pai ciang misite tho ding,
I it i ngaih lawmte tawh kimu ding;
Vantung ah ei hong paipihna dingin,
Jesuh hong paikik ding hi.
Jesuh hong pai ding a mi siangthote,
Leitung lungdamna nuam pia suk ding hi;
Bei ding hi, lungkhamna sinkhamnate,
Jesuh hong paikik ding hi.
Jesuh hong pai ding thuciamna om hi,
A teelsa mihingte la to dingin;
Ngak in, lawpin, a kisa-in om in,
Jesuh hong paikik ding hi.
=== JESUH HONG PAI BAIH DING ===
Key : Eb
Leitungah dahna tam, lungsim launa tam,
Mun tengah gal gin nam, bangcih khong ding?
Pasian kiang zuan lecin, Ama hehna panin,
Tang misiangte bangin na suakta ding.
Sakkik
Jesuh hong pai baih ding,
Sun lai maw, zan maw, zing,
Mi tampi’n gim thuak ding,
Pengkul mut ciang;
Misite thokik ding,
Midikte’n van zuan ding,
Si kik ngei nawn lo ding, vantung tun ciang.
Itna hong kiam dinga, inn le lo bei ding hi
Siatna hong tam ding a, Thubu’n gen zo;
Hih teng hong tun takteh, beina nai ding hiveh,
Pengkul mut pak ven teh, mitphiat kal in.
Gimna ong beipah ding, tawntung lungdam den ding,
Dahna om nawnlo ding hong pai ciangin;
Vantung ah leng to ning, leitung mangpha khak ning,
Amah tawh mangkhawm ding, tua hun ciangin.
=== JESUH BEK IN ===
Key : F
Aw Topa Jesuh kei lungsim
Na thu ka um man a
Sawtpi ka zong a nopna in
Lungdamna ka ngah ta
Sakkik
Tuni Jesuh sim loh inah
Deih na dang om lo pi
Itna hinna tawntung nopna
Topa kiang ka ngah hi
Lungdam na ka zon lai tak in
Topa ka mangngilh hi
Hong gum Topa ka nial ciang in
Hong it a hong zol hi
Leitung aa nop na te deih in
Lungkim ngah ding in ah
Hah kat in a ka zon hangin
Lung kiatna teng ka ngah
Jesuh hong it thupha inah
Keimah ka ngah ma in
Si thei nopna lungsim neih hang
Topa ka ngaihsun ke’n
=== JESUH AW, SINGLAMTEH KISUAN KHIN TA’NG ===
Key : Ab
Jesuh aw, Nang hong zui dingin, Singlamteh kisuan khinta’ng;
Nangma aa bek hi den dingin, simmawh muhdah thuak khinta’ng.
Ka tup, ka deih ka zonsa teng, A vekpi’n beikhinta hi;
Ahih hang ngaihsun phakik leng, Pasian na ngawn kei aa hi.
Mi’n hong simmawh, hong nusia-in, Honpa nangawn taisan hi;
Mi khempeuh ahoih bangkhemin, Nang tua bang na hi kei h i.
Itna Pasian Nangmah kong zong, Nong maitaina, kei nuamna;
Tual le galin hong taisan zong, Nong et bek zong kei nuamna.
Midangte’ hong bawlsiatna in, Na ang hong tun zawsop hi;
Leitung nuntak haksatna in, Vantung nopna hong tun hi.
Kei Na hong it lai tengin ah, Dahnate siatna’ng hilo;
Nang kihello lungdamna ah, lungnop kicing om thei lo.
Upna lum tawi, thungeninah, hehpihna tawh minthang ding;
Ka mai-a vantung nopna ah, Pasian khut in hong kha ding.
Leitung nasep bei baih dinga, Ka khualzinna bei ding hi;
Ka lam-etna tak suak dinga, Upna kimu thei ding hi.
=== JESUH AW KONG IT HI (B) ===
Key : F
Jesuh aw kong it hi, kei aa na hi ta,
Nangma hang mawhna nuam namcin ka khia ta;
Keimah hong Tanpa hong Honpa Na hi ta,
Kong it ngei leh zong, tu’n kong it ngei leh zong,
Tu’n kong it ngei leh zong, Tu’n kong it pha sem ta.
Tun’ Nang kong it hang Nang mah’n Nong it masa
Nong it ma’n singlamteh tung Nong tan zo ta,
Kong it ngei leh zong, tu’n kong it ngei leh zong,
Tu’n kong it ngei leh zong, Tu’n kong it pha sem ta.
Hong it tawntung ning hin’na sihna sung-ah,
Hong phat tawntung ning hu Nong kop lai in ah;
Sihna daitui ka tal ah kai ciangin ah,
Kong it ngei leh zong, tu’n kong it ngei leh zong,
Tu’n kong it ngei leh zong, Tu’n kong it pha sem ta.
Nuamsak tawntungna minthang innpi sungah,
Na min hong phat tawntung ning a taang van ah;
Zawhna lukhute khu in sa ning hih mah,
Kong it ngei leh zong, tu’n kong it ngei leh zong,
Tu’n kong it ngei leh zong, Tu’n kong it pha sem ta.
=== JESUH AW KONG IT HI (A) ===
Key : F
Jesuh aw kong it hi, kei aa na hi ta
Nangma hang mawhna nuam namcin ka khia ta
Keimah hong Tanpa hong Honpa Na hi ta
Kong it ngei leh zong, tu’n kong it pha sem ta.
Tun’ Nang kong it hang Nang mah’n Nong it masa

Kong it ngei leh zong tu’n kong it pha sem ta
Nuamsak tawntungna minthang innpi sungah

Zawhna lukhute khu in sa ning hih mah
Kong it ngei leh zong tu’n kong it pha sem taKey : F

Nangma hang mawhna nuam namcin ka khia ta

=== JESUH AW KA SIH DONGIN ===
Key : F
Jesuh aw, ka sih dongin, Nangma nasem dingin;
Kiciamna kip ka koihzo, Nangmah ka lawm ka To;
Hong panpih tawntung lecin, Nanglam hong hilh lecin;
Galdona kihta kei ning, lampam sikkhial kei ning.
Nangma pau hong zasak in, a siang a teltakin;
Muhnop huaite in hong leng, zaknop huaite’n hong meng;
Ka galte hong nai tawntung, ka kiim le ka lung sung;
Tuate sang hong naizaw in,
Mawhna pan hong dal in.
Nangma pau hong zasak in, A siang a teltak in;
Lungsung huihpi a nun ciang, Manglo, ka phunno ciang;
Ka lungmuan theih na’ngin-ah, Nong sawlna, nong khaamna;
Hong theisak hong ngaisak aw, ka lungsim hong cing aw.
Jesuh aw, nong iamzo hi, Nangmah a hong zui mi;
Nangma nasemte inah, Nang tawh mang ding, van-ah;
Jesuh aw, ka kiciamzo, sih dong Nangmah ka to;
Kong zuih zawh na’ng hong huh in, Ka lawm, ka Topa in.
Na khekhap, hong musak in, keimah hong tawnsak in;
Kong zuih theih na’ng mantakpi, Nangma tha kong muang hi;
Hong pi, hong sam, hong kaita’n, A tawp dong hong lenta’n;
Vantung dong hong tonpih aw, Hong hon ka Lawmpa aw.
=== JESUH ANG MUANHUAI SUNGAH ===
Key : G
Gal omlo Jesuh ang sung, kham khut tawh hong kawi ding,
Hong itna a liim beel leng, ka lungsim nuamsa ding.
Ngai un, vantung mi aw in, A vangtang vantungah;
Mual tung, tuipi tal panin, la sa bang hong tunga.
Sakkik
Gal omlo Jesuh ang sung, Kham khut tawh hong kawi ding;
Hong itna a liim beel leng, Ka lungsim nuamsa ding.
Gal omlo Jesuh ang sung, gimna tawlna beina,
Leitung ze-etna khialhna’n, Hong zolzo nawn lo ding.
Lungkiatna le dahnate, kihtakn zong dai hi;
Leitungah khitui luanna, neukha bek om lai hi.
Ka bukna Jesuh suangpi, kei tang ding hong si pa,
Tua khang suangpi ka bel a, ka muang tawntung ding hi.
Zan khuamial hun bei mateng,
Hiah ka ngak hithiat hi;
Kham khua a hong vak mateng, lungdamin ka ngak hi.
=== JESUH AH DEIHNA TENG CING HI ===
Key : Ab
Jesuh ah deihna teng cing hi
Hinna nuamna van nuai
Nisim in a matha lo in
Ka puk ding a lauhuai
Ka dah ciang Ama kiang ka pai
Mundang bang lo ka mai a taii
Ka dah ciang hong nuamsak
A mah Keima lawm
Jesuh ah deihna teng cing hi
Lungkham laitak ka lawm
Thupha deih in Amah zuan leng
A man’n hong pia nawnnawn
Nitang le guahtui hong pia hi
Tuk ciangin an hong la sak hi
Nitang guahtui le an
Hong pia keima lawm
Jesuh ah deihna teng cing hi
A tung ka thumaan ding
Kei tungah hong thumaan ka Lawm
Bang ci ka nial zo ding
Amah zui leng ka khial ngei kei
Sun le zan hong cing khial ngei kei
Sun le zan in zui ning
Amah keima lawm
Jesuh ah deihna teng cing hi
Lawmpha zaw deih tuan keng
Amah tu-in ke’n ka muang a
Muang lai ding sih mateng
Hih bang lawm tawh nuntak a nuam
Bei ngei lo ding hin’na a nuam
Bei ngei lo nuntakna nuam na
Keimah lawm
=== JESUH ADING NUNTAKNA ===
Key : F
Jesuh ading thumanin ka nungta,
A lungdamsak dingin ka hanciam a;
Lung taitakin Ama lam ka pang hi,
Thupha ka ngahna hih bang lampi hi.
Sakkik
Honpa Topa Jesuh aw, Nang tungah kong kipia,
Nong tatkhiatna dinginah, kei ading nong kipia;
To dang kuamah ka nei lo, ka lung sung hong uk in,
Nang ading bek nungta dingin, Nang tung kong kipia khin.
Ka mawhna teng Kalvary ah pua a,
Keitang si Jesuh ading ka nungta;
Tua itna in a nung hong zuisak hi,
A nungzui dingin ka kipan khin hi.
Mun khempeuh Jesuh ading ka nungta,
Amin siangtho suangin na ka sem a;
Gimna le supnate ka thuak ngam hi,
Tua bang thuakna in, kei singlamteh hi.
Tomkal nuntak Jesuh ading hi-a,
Ama nuih mai mah manpha pen ka sa;
A mangte zongin, tan ding hong si hi,
A gaimte Ama sung tawldamsak hi.
=== JESUH A MAANG DING HI ===
Key : E
Ni a taan na mun khempeuh ah,
Topa Jesuh A maang ding hi;
Lei mong khat pan mong khat dong-ah,
Ama gam in a zai ding hi.
Minam kim leh pau nam kim in,
Hong itna la in sa uh hi;
Naupangte in Amah phat in,
Ama min a thang sak ding hi.
Ama tungah thu kingen in,
Amah kiphat tawntung ding hi;
Zing meihal paknamtui bang in,
Ama’ min a kizeel ding hi.
Tua ciang minam khempeuhte in,
Ei kumpipa phat ding uh hi;
Vantung mite’n la hong sa in,
Lei mi’n “Amen” ci’n dawng ding hi.
=== JERUSALEM KHAM KHUAPI ===
Key : C
Jerusalem kham khuapi, bawngnawi khuaizu luanna,
Nangmah kong ngaih sutsut ciang,
Ke’n lamdang lua ka sa;
Keima ading lungdamna, tua lai tampi om hi,
Gen zawh loh minthanna teng,
Tua lai-ah kicing hi.
Zion innpi nuam sungah, bawlsiatna thuakte le,
Puanpak silh van mite in, phatna la sa khawm veh;
David Tokhom omna ah, gimna tawlna bei hi,
Galzo mite nuamin ah, Nuamna la sa uh hi.
Amaute in Topa tawh, galdo-in zo uh hi,
A tawntung kikhel lo-in, puanpak a silh uh hi;
Tua lai dahna omlohna, kilemna mun gam nuam,
Paakte a palh zihziahna, nuntakna innpi nuam.
Thupha a dim gam nuam pen, Pasian’ mite omna,
Thupha a dim gam nuam pen, mihingte lam-etna;
Jesuh in hong hehpih a, tua gam nuam hong tun hi,
Kha Siangtho thupha sanna, Pasian tawh omna hi.

=== ITNA KUMPI KEI HONG CINGPA ===
Key : G

Amah’n hong huh lah ngei lo;
A mi suak leng deihna cingta,
Amah kei aa hi den.

Tatsa kei hong paipih hi;

Vantung an in hong vaak hi.

Sihna ka kihta kei hi;

Singlamteh in hong pi hi.
Ka khantawnin ka nuntak sung,
Kei nong cing khial ngei kei hi;
Tuucing pha aw, Na innpi sung,
Phatna la kong sa ding hi.

=== INN AH AN LATE KHAWM DING ===
Key : Bb
Khamgam nuam panin la aw na za hiam?
Lungdamna la thak a hi;
Lawp takin buhlomte hen khawm ve ni,
A hun sawt nawnlo ding hi.
Sakkik
An la Topa tu’n hong kilang baih ding,
Amai mu-in A aw i za ding;
An la Topa tu’n hong kilang baih ding,
Innah an l ate khawm ding.
Khamgam nuam panin hong ensuk uha,
I it i lawm ngaihte hi;
Nasep khempeuh zo, Singlamteh puazo,
Khapsa lukhu khu uh hi.
Khamgam nuam panin la ngaih hong kisa,
I lungsim hong hatsak hi;
Tua la ngaih aw in, hong thakhauhsak a,
Sun niloh na i sem hi.
Khamgam nuam panin la ngaih hong kisa,
Lungnopna gam nuam pan hi;
Upna tawh i thei, a sawt lo in-ah,
Tua la i sa khawm ding hi.
=== INN PHA BEL AH I PAI DING ===
Key : Ab
Mi siangthote pai nading lampi in,
Pasian mai-ah a om ding hi;
Vantung khua mual ah i pai ngit nget a,
Zingsol i tungah hong taang hi.
Sakkik
Inn pha bel-ah i pai ding a,
Lungdamna tawh i kimu ding hi;
Khuamun nuambel eite’n i phak ciang,
Dahna om nawn lo hi.
Lam nuam tawn mi siangtho honpite in,
Zion khua a ciah kik bangin;
Meivak sungah namgim tui thun khol un,
Vantung khua ah i pai ding hi.
Lam nuam tawn ding a i ngaihsut leh,
Khat le khat i ki-itna in;
Pasian tawh eite i omkhawm dinga,
Nuam in i om tawntung ding hi.
Jordan gun gei a a votna gei-ah,
I din hangin a gal khat-ah;
Topa Pasian tawh i ngap khawm dinga,
A min i phat tawntung ding hi.
=== IHMU LENG KHANG MACIP LO IN ===
Key : C
Ihmu leng khangma cip loin, minthanna khua hong vak ding;
Hinkik ni ciang kimu kik leng, i kikhen nawn kei ding hi.
Tuipi thuk le kuam thuk sung pan, minam cin hong khawm ding hi,
Mual dawn, mual kuam, gamlak panin, mi tampi hong tho ding hi.
Sakkik
Ihmu leng khangma cip lo-in, minthanna khuavak ding hi,
Hin kik ni ciang kimu kikin, I kikhen nawn kei ding hi.
Paak hoih banga i deih mahmah, I lung hihmawh phat mahmah;
I ang sung pan i lakkhiat ciang, lian mahmah hi i dahna,
Ni a tum dek matengin ah, han kiim ah i kunkun a,
Eite’n paak i it manin ah, lam-etna bei bang kisa.
Ihmu leng khangma cip lo-in, han sungah lumcip lo ding;
Hong sap ciangin thupha a pia, Topa’n thupha ngah tahen,
Sihna om ngei nawn lohna mun, a kip tawntung khuapi ah,
Omna inn nuam ngah dingin-ah, Topa in hong sam ding hi.
=== I TOPA HONG ITNA LAMDANG HI ===
Key : G
I Topa hong itna lamdang hi
Mawhna, khialhna i neih hang tampi,
Lian zaw tham lai hong hehpih na si,
Kalani mual tung ah hong bua hi
Sakkik
Hong hehpih na, i mawhna
hong maisak, siangsak hi, Pasian itna,
I mawhna teng sangin lian zaw hi
Mawhna lungkiat na’n tui khang bang in.
Ka kha hong sut nuam hong to laitak,
Gen zawh loh lian zaw hehpih na in,
Ka belh ding Singlamteh pi hong lak
Kiseelzo nawn kei i mawhna nin,
Bang a om diam hong sawp zo lai ding,
En un, hia-a luang sisan gunpi’n,
Vuk sang hong ngo zaw sak pah thei ding
Lamdang kicing hehpihna lian zaw,
A um khempeuh A hong piak khong hi,
A mai a mu nuamte khempeuh aw,
Saang pak ve un hong hehpih na hi.
=== IH THEIH NA DING HI ===
Key : F
Buaina haksatna, i tuah ciangin ah,
Bang hang hizahta ke’n thuakse a;
Ka kiim ka paam a, misiate in lah,
Bangmah thuakse lo, lamdang ka sa.
Sakkik
Nung ciang a vekpi’n i thei nading hi,
Nung ciang a hang i telna ding hi;
Na lung nuamsak in, nitang sung om in,
Nung ciang a vekpi’n i tel ding hi.
It le ngaihte tawh sihna’n hong khen ciang,
I inn sung hawmin i lung zuang a;
A gilo mite, a dau a pai ciang,
Bang hang tua ci hiam? lamdang i sa.
Sih dong thuman in, Topa in hong ci,
Tawl khat sung ngak in, thuak lai leteh;
Na gim na tawlna, gentham lo ding hi,
Et lawm kongpi sung na luttak teh.
Min thannapi tawh vantung inn panin,
Jesuh hong kumsuk i mu ding hi,
A tang inpi sung i omkhop ciangin,
Telloh khempeuh i telta ding hi.

A ma thu khenna maan te mei taang kiaukiau ah sim thei ing
I Pasian mai nawt hi
Nungkik ding a, sam ngei lo ding peengkul Amah’n mut hi
A thu khen na tokhom maiah mi hing te lungsim sit hi
Ka kha aw, amah dawng meng in! nuam in, ka khe!
Nuam huai hi I Pasian mai nawt hi
Tuipi gal khat, unok paak hoih lakah Khazih suak khin hi.
Nang le kei hong kikheel sak A ang sung
minthan’na tawi hi.
Mite siangsak ding hong sih bangin,
mi’ suahtak nang si ni. Pasian mai nawt lai hi
=== I PA HONG HEHPIHNA MEIVAK ===
Key : Bb
I Topa hong hehpihna in,
Suum pempam in hong tang hi;
Tua khuavak eite hong pia hi,
Tui tung teng ah tangsak in,
Sakkik
Meivak teng a vek pi’n vaak in,
Tuihual teng kimuh nading;
A cimawh tuikia om kha ding,
Gum khia in-la kaikhia in.
Mawhna in khua hongmial sak hi,
Tui-hualpi hong kilok hi;
Hoih takin khuadak pha in-la,
Tui dung teng phatak en in.
Na meivak phatak vak inla,
Tuihual in mi taai kha ding;
Nop takin suahtak theih nading,
Tawl ngakna mun tun theih nang.

A kiang i tung ding hi.

=== HUN NUAM MAH MAH ===
Key : F
Phatna thungetna hun nuam hi, Pasian i biakkhop ciang;
Ama kiangah lengto ding hi, Nuamna la i sak ciang.
Kamciam manpha hong kipiata, I telsiang semsem ding;
Lei-ah lawmte tawh kikhen hang, Van-ah kimu kik ding.
Sakkik
Ni tawp ni ciang eite khempeuh
Van-ah i kimu ding;
Jesuh’ sipha i upna hang,
Vanah kimu kik ding.
Eite lungsim hong kihualsak, Itna siangtho hi-a;
Pasian Topa Khris min hangin, Eite i kikhawmta.
Kikhenna hun hong tun baih hang, A thuciam kip hi;
“Eite lam-etna vantungah, Kimukik ding” hong ci.
A gim, atawl i khete in, Khamgam sik baih ding hi;
I it i lawmte hong ngakna, tua kham gam nuam sung hi.
Kum kivei lo tom kal sungin, Huihpi tuihual ven ciang;
Tawntung lungdamna la sa ding, van ah i kimuh ciang.
=== HUIHPI NUN CIANGA KIDALNA ===
Key : F
I bukna suangpi Topa hi, Huihpi nun ciang a kidalna;
A sia namkim a’ ding bit hi, Huihpi nun ciang a kidalna.
Sakkik
Gimna gam sungah Jesuh Suangpi a hi!
Belh ding Suangpi, Belh ding suangpi;
Gimna gam sungah Jesuh Suangpi a hi,
Huihpi nun ciang a kidalna!
Sunin ni lim, zan in kulh pi, Huihpi nun ciang a kidal na;
Kihtak ding gal om nawn lo hi, Huihpi nun ciang a kidal na.
Huihpi’n i kiimkot nuai hang in, Huihpi nun ciang a kidalna;
Nusia lo ding cik mah hun in, Huihpi nun ciang a kidalna.
Pasian Suangpi, belh ding it huai, Huihpi nun ciang a kidalna;
Tawntung hong nai, hong kem, hong huai, Huihpi nun ciang a kidalna.
=== HUIHPI NAKPI’N A ANUN SIMIN ===
Key : C
Huihpi nakpi’n a nun simin,
Dahna tui bang a khan simin;
Zuat ding tawldam huai, lungmuan huai;
Mun om, hehpihna tokhom nuai.
Eite i lu tungah Jesuh’n,
Lungdam sathau hong nilhna mun;
Mundang teng sang nuam pen mun om,
Sisan baang hehpihna tokhom.
Kha le khat lungsim kigawmna,
Lawm le gual tawh kikholh theihna;
Kikhen hang pum khat bang hong suah,
Hehpihna tokhom kiim kituah.
Pumpi’ utna le mawhnate’n,
Hong nawngkaisakzo nawn lo ding;
Vantung in hong dawntuah sukta,
Vangtang in tua tokhom tuam ta.
=== HUIHPI A VEN MATENG ===
Key : Eb
Zankim khuamial laitakin lau-in ka buzel a,
Ka tungah huihpi nungin, ka belh ding lah thei keng;
Hih van ginna phual panin, hong ngai in, kong thuumna,
“Hong kem in huihpi a ven mateng.”
Sakkik
Huihpite veng mang khina, vangingte a beisiang dong,
Van a meiite beimang a khua phat dong;
Topa, hong len in na khut kuak sung hong koih in,
Hong kem in huihpi a ven mateng.
Hahkat hang a mawkna pi, dahna bei theilo pi,
Lam-etna zong om beek kei ci’n Satan’n hong khem hi;
A’ih hang Nong ompih thei ing, zing ciang thoto inah,
“Ka pai ding huihpi omlohna ah.”
Zan saupi bei khinta a huihpi a ven ciangin,
Na mai-ah ka ding ding hi, tua a tang gungei-ah;
Tua gamah huihpi omlo hong teng ning Topa aw,
“Huihpi a ven khittak ciangin maw.”
=== HUHPA HONG PAI KHIN TA ===
Key : C
Lungdam thu zeel-sak un, mi omna ci tengah,
Mihing lungsim omna mihing gal tamna ah,
Tapidaw leii khempeuh lungdam thugensak un.
Huhpa hong pai khinta.
Sakkik
Huhpa hong pai khinta,
Vantung Kha Siangtho pen,
Pa’n piak ding hong ciam pen,
Lungdam thu zeel sak un.
Mi omna ci tengah;
Huhpa hong pai khinta.
Zan hun saupi beita, mi omna citeng ah,
Lungsim vangikpi teng, hehna huging vengta;
Nitang khammual pan in hong suahkhiat tak ciang in,
Huhpa hong pai khinta.
A kha sung zatui tawh, kumpi te’ To hat pa’n,
Thongkia kha khempeuh tung, hong puak, hotkhiat kicing;
Thongpi hawm sung teng ah, zawhna lapi hong ging;
Huhpa hong pai khinta.
Genzawh loh itna siang! ka leii in bang ci-in,
Genzawh loh hehpihna, mi vakvai tung gen ding;
A mah le A meel tang, sungah ka om theihna’ng;
Huhpa hong pai khinta.
Awging van khum dawnah, leng in thawn to sak un;
Vantung misiangte’aw, leinuai mi dawng sak un;
Tatsat lo itna sung, a bei ngeilo ding la;
Huhpa hong pai khinta.
=== HUAN SUNGAH ===
Key : Ab
Pak tung zingdai a nom lai-in,
Keimah guak huan sungah ka vak hi;
Hong kihopihna ka zak aw ging in,
Pasian Tapa’ awkhum hi.
Sakkik
Amah’n hong tonpih-in hong hopih a,
Ama aa ka hih hong gen hi;
Amah tawh omkhawm a nuam ka sakna,
Kuamah’n ciam kha ngei lo hi.
Hong hopihna khum mahmah a,
Vasate’n zong ngai khipkhep uh hi;
Kei a hong sak tua la ngaih mahmah a,

=== HONG LIAH IN ===
Key : Ab

A kip tawntung Sungpi pha aw, Hong liah in.

Topa aw ka lungmuanna ding, Hong liah in.

A kip tawntung Sungpi pha aw, Hong liah in.
Dahna khua a hong mial lai teng, Hong liah in!
Minthan ni zing khuavak mateng, Hong liah in.
Jordan gunpi gei ka nai ciang,
Na ang muanhuai sung kong tun ciang;
A kip tawntung Suangpi pha aw, Hong liah in.
=== HONG KISIN DIH UN ===

Sakkik

Thupha kong pia ding, kong daupai sak ding,
Thupha a tampi kong pia ding hong i.

Meigong nu sumpi piak bangin pia un;
A sia thei lo vantungah na sum khol un,
Pasian hoihna thupha na zeek ding hi.
Ka Biakinn ah, an a om theih nadingin,
Sawm ah khat a kimin hong paipih un;
Vantung kongkhakte hongin note ading,
Na hoih tampi kong piakna na mu ding hi.

=== HI NING ===
Key : A
Kei hong Honpa thu-in kong kipia a,
Suahtakna kcing hi;
Tun ka lungsim khentat phamawh ta,
Kong tang ta diam, ka ci.
Sakkik
Hi ning! Hi ning! Pasian aw nong huh hi,
Nang aa bek hong hi ning,
Nong tatkhiatna’ng, Na si manpha luang hi,
Nang aa bek hong hi ning.
Tu-in Topa, Nang kong sang nuamta hi,
Na itna’n hong zota;
Khris Topa aw, Nang kong beel nuamta hi,
Nangmah bek kong muangta.
Ka thanemna, lam pial ding ka launa,
Topa aw nong thei hi;
Na nasep na’ng hong guan in thahatna,
Nang bek kong mitsuan hi.
Na hehpihna tu’n hong pia in, Topa,
La-in ka sasa ding;
Lungdam takin tu’n ka genkhia dinga,
“Khris aa bek hi’ng” ci ning.
Leitung na om lai-a hong zuante in,
“Topa nong sem diam” ci;
“Kong sem nuam hi” ci-a Na dawnna in,
Kote’ lungmuanna hi.
=== HEHPIHNA’N HONG GUM ===
