Hong lut sak ding hiam khawlna-ah.
Ni khat ni ding vil in ngak in,

=== HEHPIHNA A NGEN TE ===

Sepzawh na’ngtha hongpia ding Topa in;
A kaw-cik lampi ah,
Zol teitei in-la,
Hilh in a ma’ tang Topa si khin ta.
=== ANI ANI IN NGAIH SEMSEM ===
Key : D
A deihhuai tangthu Hon pa itna thu,
Ani ani-in ngaih semsem;
Hong khap sa van inn hang lung-muanna thu,
Ani ani-in ngaih semsem.
Sakkik
A ni (ani) simin, Amah (amah) phatna la sasa ni,
Hun zong nuam semsem (nuam semsem);
Van a Pasian i phatna la,
Ani a ni-in ngaih semsem.
Nuntakna khuavak pan a vang tangpi,
Ani ani-in tang semsem;
Dahna hong hehnem kamciam na aksi,
Ani a ni-in tang semsem.
Huihpi nung ciang a hong len sikkippi,
Ani ani-in kip semsem;
Nuntak tawntungna thu i theita hi,
Ani ani-in thei semsem.
Jesuh in eite hong piak lungnopna,
Ani ani-in nuam semsem;
Khristiante a’ ding kihong lam-etna,
Ani ani-in nuam semsem.
=== AN LAKPHAT KHINTA HI ===
Key : Ab
An lak phat khin ta hi, Kuai khin zota hi,
Khris Topa’n hong sam a ni bei baih ding hi;
Hong sawl bang sem meng in, An-late pawm in,
Tha nuamtak sem in la an-late huh in.
Sakkik:
An lak phat khin ta hi, sep theih lai sem in;
A hun bei han han hi, Tuni-in sem in.
An lak phat khin ta hi, Kihei hei kei in,
An late sepna aw huih in hong puak khin;
Lungduai takin sem in, Khawm in anvui teng,
Kham leh zang mun khempeuh ni hong tum mateng.
An lak phat khin ta hi, Tuni’n kua kuan ding?
An late huh in buhlomte kuan pua ding;
Na kisep theih sun hun, Hong bei baih ding hi,
Na zawh ciang Topa’n “Pha hi” hong ci ding hi.
=== AMAH’N HONG KHA ===
Key : D
Amah’n hong kha hih thu mahmah, hehnepna ding thupha a hi,
Ka sepna ka paina teng ah Pasian khut in kei hong kha hi.
Sakkik
A mah’n hong kha Amah’n hong kha,
Ama khut tawh A mah’n hong kha,
A nung mantak ka zui ding hi,
Ama khut in kei hong kha hi.
Khatvei leh Eden bang nuamna,
Khatvei leh khuamialna thukpi,
Bang ka tuak hang muanna launa,
Ka Pasian in kei hong kha hi.
Phunlo puamlo lungkim takin,
Topa na khut ka len nuam hi.
Bangbang tuak zong bang lungkhamna,
Ka Pasian in kei hong kha hi.
Na hehpihna tawh galzo a
Nasep ka khit ciang a vekpi’n;
Sih ding lau lo Pasian in ah,
Jordan gungal ah hong kha hi.
=== AMAH MUANG IN ===
Key : G
Mawhna a neite hong pai in
Topa in hong hehpih
A ma thupha bel up ciang in
Nuamna i ngah ding hi
Sakkik
A mah muang in, A mah muang la
Tu in ah muang in
Hong gum ding hi, hong gum ding hi
Tu in hong gum ding
Nuamna a hong pia ding Jesuh
A si pha bel luang sak
Vuk sang in hong ngo zaw sak thei
A si sung hong phum ta’n
Nop na sung tun’ na ding
Jesuh Thumaan lam pi a hi
Topa na um ding khawl kei leh
Lung dam na ngah ding hi
Mi siang tho kikhopna mun leh
Min thanna mun pai ni;
Lung dam om tawn tung na sung ah
Nuamna i ngah ding hi
=== AMAH MANPHA ===
Key : A
Lungsim siansuah leng, Topa biakinnpi hi a,
Hong ompihna i thei hi;
Ama min suangin kikhawm leng nuam mahmah a,
Siangtho thunget hun nuam hi.
Sakkik
A umte khempeuh ading Amah manpha,
A sangte khempeuh ading Amah manpha,
Topa’ min a kikhop ciang,
Genkhia ni Ama thupha,
I thungetna hong dawng ding.
Ama min thanna khuavakpi hong tang suk hi,
I lam-etna a neu ciang;
A tate ngah ding itna lian tampi om hi,
Amah tawh i tonkhop ciang
Hong paipihna peuh zui leng Amah’n hong paakta,
I lung sung nopna dim hi;
I kimkot tengah tawntung khut in hong huai a,
I upna tawh i thei hi.
Kumpi inn sungah lungnop tawntungna munah
Lungdamna khutbet ma teng;
Thutak thei tel in khangcing ni hehpihna ah,
Nopna kicing luah khawm leng.
=== A ZOZO HI ===
A neu a lian kua cilo, mawh, mawh lo ci lo;
Jesuh’n vekpi ading khin, sawtpi pek in-ah.
Sakkik
A zozo hi! Takpi hi, vekpi’n zokhin hi;
Hih hi, mawh neite i sap, mawhna pulak ding.
Sang pen a tokhom tung pan, kum in hong sih ciang;
Na khempeuh a vekin zo, A aw ngai dih un.
Lunggim van pua nasemte’n, koi-ah sem na hiam?
Khawl dih in Amah’n zozo, sawtpi pek inah.
Na vangikpi teng khia in, Jesuh khe kiang khia’n;
Amah bekbek kiang ding in, Na khempeuh cinkhin.
Jesuh nasepsa muang in, na up theih mateng;
Hanciamna in kimanglo, sihna hong tunzaw.
=== A UT KHEMPEUH TE ===
Key : D
A zate khempeuh in hih thu tangko un,
Leitung khempeuh ah hih thupha thangsak un;
Mi na muh khempeuh hih nuamna thu ko un,
A ut khempeuh hongpai thei
Sakkik
“A ut khempeuhte,” “A ut khempeuhte,”
Cih na thu a mual a guam va thawn sak un;
Hong it i Pa in hong samkik lam khialte,
“A ut khempeuh hong pai un.”
Hong paite in zekai
nading thu om lo,
Lut theih lai in lut un,
Kong hon sa’n om zo;
Jesuh lo thu man
hinna lampi om lo,
A ut khempeuh hong pai thei
A ut khempeuhte
thuciam a man tak hi,
A ut khempeuhte
thuciam a kip ding hi;
A ut khempeuh-te”
nuntak tawntung na hi,
A ut khempeuh hong pai thei
=== A THUSIAM PEN PASIAN ===
Key : D
A thusiam pen Pasian aw, deih teng cinna Na hi;
Na nuntakna laigil tawh, Amaute Na gawm hi.
Sih dongin a amau tegel, A thuciam uh kip hen;
Na vangliatna tawh kigeel, Na thupha sang uh hen.
Leitungah Na om lai-in, Kana Na pai laitak;
Kiteenna pawi va simin, Tui lengtui na suaksak.
Tua lai mopina pawi a, Na thupha hong tung hen.
Nangmah hong muan theih nangun, Topa aw, Na huh in;
Haksatna a thuak ciangun, Na ompih tawntung in.
Leitung a nusiat ni dong, Nang sungah kip uh hen;
Na innpi ah hong tun dong, Nangmah hong muang uh hen.
=== A THU KA GENGEN NUAM HI ===
Key : Ab
A thu ka gengen nuam hi,
Muh nai-loh vantung na;
Jesuh leh Ama vangpi,
Jesuh leh hongit-na
Thu ka gengen nuam hi,
Thuman ahih manin;
Ka lungsim hong kim sak hi,
Thu dangte bang lo-in.
Sakkik:
Tua thu ka gen-gen nuam hi,
Gengen lai ning vantungah;
Hih thu tul thei ngei lo pi,
Jesuh le hong itna.
A thu ka gengen nuam hi,
Lamdang semsem ka sa;
Kingaihsun thei nawn lopi,
Tua sang lamdangzaw na;
Tua thu ka gengen nuam hi, Hong nop-tuamsak na lian;
Tua hang mah’n kong gen sawn hi, Tu in lawm aw, nang kiang.
A thu ka gengen nuam hi,
Gengen leng nuam semsem;
Ka gengen sa hi napi,
Gengen leng ngaih semsem;
Tua thu ka gengen nuam hi,
Hotkhiatna thu a pha;
A za nai lo mi om hi,
Pasian hong gen thupha.
A thu ka gengen nuam hi,
A thei pente in zong;
An duh tuiduh bang duh hi,
Midangte sang in zong;
Vantung vanliatna sungah,
La thak ka sa ding hi;
Tua ciangin hih thului mah,
Kei in ka sa ding hi.
=== A TANG TAWNTUNGNA MUN ===
Key : Bb
Tua lai gam om nitum lohna,
Van ah ni tang tawntung;
Tua lai nitak om ngei lo hi,
Topa vang in tang hi.
Sakkik
Singlamteh e’n i puak leh,
Kham lukhu i khu ding;
Mi hoihte sung i ten leh,
Khuavak sung i om ding.
Tua lai mun om kilemna gam,
Gimna om nawnlohna;
Tua lai huih dam zong nung hiauhiau,
I tunna’ng tua mun-ah.
Tua lai inn om, minthang inn om,
A kigen van inn nuam;
I tun nading vantung inn nuam,
Ei hong dawn ding tua lai.
I pum lui na i nusiat leh,
Manlangin hong kheng ding,
A tang van zinpa kiang zuan leng,
I lung nuam tawntung ding.
=== A SINGLAMTEH KE’N VELVEL LENG ===
Key : Eb
Vanglian Kumpipa hong sihna,
A singlamteh ke’n velvel leng
Kei’ hauhna kei kiphat sakna,
Ke’n tu’n bangmah in sim nawn keng
Khazih ka Pasian sihna lo,
Kisialhpih ding bangmah om kei;
Ka deih bel teng khat zong siit lo,
Ama’ si khekna in ka nei.
En ven, a lu a khut, akhe,
Dahna, itna hong luang suk khawm;
Na mu ngei maw linglukhu le,
Itna, dahna gawm kilawm khawm.
Leitung khempeuh pia thei hileng,
Tamlua ka ci ngei kei ding hi;
A hong itna ke’n ngaihsun leng,’
Ka pum ka tak ka pia nuam hi.
=== A SAWT LOIN INN-AH CIAH DING ===
Key : F
Lampi ah hong lungnuam sak ding la khat sa ni,
A sawt loin ah inn ah ciah ding;
Zan khuamial bei ding, ni tang tawntungna sungah,
A sawt loin ah inn ah ciah ding.
Sakkik
A sawt loin ah, a sawt loin ah,
Tuipi hual i kantan ding;
Eite kimu ding huihpi nung a ven ciang in,
A sawt loin ah inn ah ciah ding.
Sep ding i muh peuh i khut in i sem ding hi,
A sawt lo inah inn ah ciah ding;
Pasian hehpihna in i tha hong khauhsak ding,
A sawt lo inah inn ah ciah ding.
A gim khete a’ ding lam i sialsak ding hi,
A sawt loin ah inn ah ciah ding;
Itna lungsim kizel kim in hoih na lawh hen!
A sawt loin ah inn ah ciah ding.
Lungkhamna peng in tawldamna gal khat-ah om,
A sawt loin ah inn ah ciah ding;
Tua khuapi nuam sungah khitui luanna om lo,
A sawt loin ah inn ah ciah ding.
=== A SANNA LAM KA KAHTO HI ===
Key : Ab
A sang na lam ka kah to hi
Ni sim a thak ka tung to hi
Kah to kawm kong thum lai Topa
Hong suan to aw a sang zaw ah
Sakkik
Topa aw hong domto in la,
Ka muh ngeinai loh van zang ah
Up na tawh ong ding to sak in
A sang zaw ah ong suan to in
Lung manna launa tamna ah
Midang te a ut hang in ah
Kei ka lungsim a ut kei hi
Kei tupna a sang zaw na hi
A sang zaw a mi siangte’ la
Upna tawh kei mah in ka za
Dawi mangpa’n thal in hong kap hang
Ka sang zaw nuam hi leitung sang
A sang pen dong ka kah nuam hi
Vanglian a tang ka mu nuam hi
Vantung ka muh dong Topa aw
A sang zaw ah hong pi to aw
=== A NUAM KUMPI INN SUNG AH ===
Key : Eb
Anuam kumpi inn sungah i om zongin,
Ei inn sang a nuamzaw inn dang omlo hi;
“Hiah inn nuam om hi” van pan hong ci zongin,
Ei inn sanga nuamzaw inn dang omlo hi
Sakkik
Inn nuam, inn nuam pen, ei inn kan om kei
Eima inn mah nuam pen.
Gamlak ka vak kawmin khapi ka en a,
Ka nu’n a ta hong phawk lamtak ka thei hi;
Kong gei paak kiang pan khapi na en-en a,
Tua paak namtui ka dikkha nawn kei ding hi.
Inn pan taikhiat hang mun nuam dang omlopi,
Ka bukno khiukheu mahah hong tunkik in;
Kei hong lungnuamsak vasate’n la sa hi.
=== A NISIM IN KHUM SEM SEM ===
Key : Bb
Nisim ka nuntakna Jesuh tawh kinai semsem veng,
Ngun le kham sang siangzaw tang zaw, A hoihna genzo keng;
Ka lungsim mit kha in Ama hoihna teng ka mu hi,
Nisim hunsim khangto Jesuh itna khum semsem hi.
Sakkik
Kim khat beek kigenzo kei,
Tua galkhat kham khua thu;
Jesuh hong itna khumzaw tham lai ding hi, tua mun ah.
A gamla pek pan ka mu hi, A vangliatna hong tang,
Unok pak sang hoihzaw tham lai, zingsol bangin hong taang;
Ka lunggulhnate hong pia in, kei hong lungkimsak hi,
Nisim hunsim khangto Jesuh itna khum semsem hi.
Lungkhamna ka thuakzelzel hang, Amah’n hong suakta sak,
A ang sung hong pom hong dal in, ka lungkhamna beisak;
Kei tang ding A pumpi’n hong thuakna hang Khris ka it hi,
Nisim hunsim khangto Jesuh itna khum semsem hi.
=== A NUNG CIANGIN KIMUKIK DING ===
Key : A
I kimuh na’ng gun galkhat ah,
Nung ciangin, nung ciangin;
Khuamial hun om ngei loh-na ah,
Nung ciangin, nung ciangin;
Khuazin gimna bei khin a,
Minthanna tawh galzo in;
Ni bangin i tang ding hi,
Nung ciangin, nung ciangin.
Minthanna guasem i tum ding,
Nung ciangin, nung ciangin;
Ei hong gupna la i sa ding,
Nung ciangin, nung ciangin;
A kisia ngeilo vantung,
Lungdam nopsak den-na mun;
Gun gal thawm in la sa ding,
Nung ciangin, nung ciangin.
Jesuh mu in kibang ta ding,
Nung cingin, nung ciangin;
Kisia thei lo lukhu ngah ding,
Nung ciangin, nung ciangin;
A kisia ngei lo vantung,
Vantung mi nasemte in;
Ei’ na hong sep sak ding hi,
Nung ciangin, nung cingin.
Khitui luanna om nawn lo ding,
Nung ciangin, nung ciangin;
Lungdamna nuam pen hi ta ding,
Nung ciangin, nung ciangin;
A paisa mi siangthote,
Nuntakna gam nuam tungta;
Amau tawh awng ding eite,
Nung ciangin, nung ciangin.
=== A NUAM INN ===
Key : G
Vantung gam lam i zuat nadingin,
Jesuh in lam hong sialsak zo ta;
I gal khempeuh a vekpi’n zo khin,
Hih lam-ah hong pai un u le nau.
Sakkik
Gam nuamah om ding in, om dingin, om dingin,
Hih lam-ah hong pai un u le nau,
Gam nuamah om dingin, om dingin, om dingin,
Hih lam-ah hong pai un u le nau.
Tu-inah hehpihna lam zong un,
Tua hi leh khuamialna bei ding hi;
A umte in vantung gam zuan un,
Na up leh vantung na tung ding hi.
Jesuh in hong hehpih in hong sam,
A um lo mite umsak ding hi;
Hehpihna thupha ngah ding hong sam,
Pasian gam sung hong lutpih ding hi.
=== A NAI, A GAMLA LOTE AH ===
Key : Ab
A nai, a gamla lote ah,
Ante min khin zo ta hi;
Simlo zo muallo zanglo ah,
Anvuite min zo ta hi.
Sakkik
Topa aw kote hong thumna,
Hong ngai in an nei Topa;
An la ding mi hong kuansak in,
An lak hun a khen ma in.
Zingsang phalvak tung ahi zong,
Sun kim ciang a hi zongin;
Hong kuan sak lai in nitak zong,
Lo laiteng ankhawm dingin.
Kuan meng un, Topa’ sawltakte,
An vuite kuaizo ta hi;
An kaikhawm khin,
ni hong tum teh,
lung damin na ciah ding hi.
=== A MANPHA PEN SUANG ===
Key : G
A manpha pen suang ke’n mu ing,
Lungdamin la ka sa;
Jesuh kei aa ci’n la sa ning,
Khazih la-in sa ning.
Sakkik
A manpha pen suang ke’n mu ing,
Lungdamin la ka sa;
Jesuh kei aa ci’n la sa ning!
Khazih la-in sa ning
Jesuh Siampi ka Kumpi hi,
Khuavak Kamsangpa hi;
Tokhom mai-ah Kamsanglian pa,
Ka van Kumpipa hi.
Amah topa-te’ Topa hi,
Kumpite’ Kumpi hi;
Amah in thumanna Ni hi,
A kha nuai cidamna.
Kilemna ding kei taang hong si,
Kei tang A si hong bua;
A lamdang kei hong gum Pa hi,
Amah mahin hong gum.
Khazih ah deihna teng cinga,
Ka lungmuanna ahi;
Leitung hinna Amah hi-a,
Vantung hinna zong hi.
=== A MANG TE ZONG HI ===
Key : Bb
A mangte hong zongin hong zol ngeungeu,
Mual sang tung a lam a khial mite;
“Keimah hong zuan un” hong cikik leuleu,
Topa’n tuni-in hong sam eite.
Sakkik
Mual sang tunga gamla ah pai ni,
A vak mite lakik ni;
Mawh nei mi tang dinga si Tuuno
I honpa’ tuubuk ah khum in.
A mangte zongin Jesuh’ lamlak in,
Thahat lo kha le a na lungsim;
Hotkhiatna lampi sungah makaih in,
Nuntak tawntungna lampi lak in.
Tua bangin pai ni thupha nasem mi,
Khazih zui den ni, a ni sialin;
A bah mi lawpsak in, pukmi phong ni,
A mang mi lampi Jesuh lak ni.
=== A MIN THANG TA HEN ===
Jesuh sihna singlamteh phungah,
Mawhna hong phel na’ng kaki ko a;
Tua lai-ah sisan in hong sawp ta,
A minthang ta hen.
Sakkik
A minthang ta hen,
A minthang ta hen;
Tua lai ah sisan in hong sawp ta,
A min thang ta hen.
Mawhna pan hong hotna lamdang hi,
Jesuh’n nuam tak-in hong om pih hi;
Tua sing lamteh ah kei hong sam hi,
A minthang ta hen.
Mawh sawp siang na tui nak manpha a,
Ka tun man in kei ka nuam lua a;
Jesuh’n hong hon hong siang sak zo ta,
A min thang ta hen.
Tua cik tui man-pha ah hong pai un,
Jesuh khe phungah hong ki-ap un;
Ki bual un-la, kisawp siang sak un,
Amin thang ta hen.
=== A MANPHATNA GEN THEI HI LENG ===
Key : Eb
Hong hon Topa tungah a taang, A lian mahmah tawntung a vang;
Phat ding kah to thei leng, Vantung gawsemte tum khawmin;
A lamdang late sasa in, Gabriel dem nuam veng, Gabribel dem nuam veng
Mawhna pan hong tatkhiat na’ng in, Jesuh’n Asi pha hong bua khin;
Nuamna la ka sa ding, A dikna la’n sa nuam sing maw;
Vantung kizepna kicing tawh,
Ni bang ka tang den ding, Ni bang ka tang den ding.
Vanglian tokhom tungah tu a, Itna mel pua in a omna;
La in sa sa nuam ing, A liatna leh a hoih manin;
‘Angaih mahmah late sa in,
Thangsak tawntung nuam ing Thangsak tawntung nuam ing’.
Lungnop ni hong tun tak ciang, Topa’n hong ciah pih ding a kiang;
Ama mai ka mu ding, Hong hehpihna gualzawhna tawh;
Hong honpa Jesuh ka lawm tawh;
Nuamsa khawm tawntung ning, Nuamsa khawm tawntung nuam ning.
=== A MAH’N KA MAWH NA TENG LAKHIA ZO ===
Key : Bb
Lungsim leh aw in, Topa phat ning,
Ama sung ka kipak ding.
La in sa ning lamdang hong itna
Ken sasa ning hih la
Sakkik
Ama’n ka mawhna teng lakhia zo
Amin siang phat un, Amin siang phat un
Ama’n ka mawhna teng lakhia zo
Haleluijah min phat un.
Nopna khawlna ngah ding amakiang
Ka mawhna tawh ka pai ciang
Ka nget hong za in hong khahkhia ta
Ken sasa ning hih la.
Ka hu tawpna tawh Amah phat ning
Sihna ka zawh manin ah.
Amah phat ning a tawntungin ah
Ken sasa ning hih la.
=== A LAMDANG TANGTHU LASA NING ===
Key : Eb
A lamdang tangthu lasa ning
Jesuh kei taang ding si hi
Vantung min than’na nusia a
Singlamteh sih na thuak hi
Sakkik
A lamdang tangthu lasa ning
Jesuh si hi kei tang ding
Lim lang tui thuk gei ki khop ciang
Mi siangtho te tawh sa ning
A gammangte Jesuh’n zong hi
Lam a khial tuu te zong hi
A khut tawh kei mah hong pom hi
Lampi ah hong kha kik hi
Cinate Jesuh’n dam sak a
A kipukte zong phong hi
Mittaw in a lau na tam a
A hih hang hong gum ding hi
Khuamial kei tungah hong tung ta
Dahna lampi ka zui ta
Kei hong ompih in Topa aw
Hong keem in lam hong hilh ta
Sihna gun gal kah mateng in
Topa in hong cing ding hi
I itte tawh kimu ding in
Gungal ah hong kha ding hi
=== A LUNGDAMTE HONG PAI UN ===
A lungdamte hong pai un, An lakna la hong sa un;
Phalbi guahsia zukma in, An khempeuh kikaikhawm khin;
I kisapna khempeuhte, Pasian in hong pia eite;
Biakinnpi ah hongpai un, An-lakna la hong sa un.
Leitung khempeuh Pasian’lo, Amah phatna’ng ankung po;
Tang le tahum hong pokhawm, Nuamna, dahna hongkhang khawm;
Teh neih khit ciang hong gah a, A nung ciangin hong tak sa;
An nei Topa in Na lo, Ko nong hah ding kong ngen zo.
Lo ah Topa hongkuan ding, Inn-ah ante ciahpih ding;
Tua ni ciang i Topa in, An si seep ding lo panin;
Van-mite thupia inah, Tahumte kikhul ding a;
A taksa teng kaikhawm ding, A tawntungin nuamsa ding.
Hong pai meng in Topa aw, Innah hong ciahpih ta aw;
Na mite hong kaikhawm in, Mawhna dahna pan khah in;
A tawntung a siangtho ding, Nangmah tawh omkhawm den ding;
Van mite tawh hong pai aw, Innah hong ciah pih ta un.
=== A LIAN PEN KUMPIPA ===
Key : G
A hong kumsuk Topa
Na min phat na ding la
Ko hong pia in
Vanglian minthang Topa
Leitung kheem peuh zo a
Hong pai hong uk in la
Bei sa ni tawh
Biakna nuamna hong pia
Kote’ thu hong nget na
Na hong ngai in
Lam khial nei mite in
Thumuh kikna ding in
Lam hilh ding hong pai in
Kha Siangtho aw
Thu hilh Kha Siangtho aw
Hilh ding hong pai in la
Tu’n hong pai aw
Siamna a om khempeuh
Kha Siangtho om khempeuh
Ko tungah hong pia’n la
Hong uk ta aw
Nam thum pawl khat Pasian
Topa nangmah a lian
Na minthang hen
Vantung gam sung nang mah
Na vanglian mi dingin
Nangmah a tawntung in
Ka it ding hi
=== A KIGELH HIAM KA MIN ===
Key : Ab
Topa hauhna ngaihsun ke’ng, kham le ngun lunggulh ke’ng;
Vantung gam cian masa ning, Tuu huang sung lut nuam ing;
Vantung gam laipi sungah, Na ciamtehna sungah;
A kigelh hiam, keima min? Jesuh aw hong gen in.
Sakkik:
Gam ciamtehna sungah, nuntakna lai sungah,
Vantung ka tun theih na’ngin, A kigelh hiam ka min
(v3 Kigelh mah hi, ka min)
Gungei-a sehnel bangin, ka mawhna tam hangin,
Topa aw, Nong tatna si, kei ading kicing hi;
Na thuciamtehna laipi, mual theilo ding taang hi;
“Na mawhsi bang san hangin, paaksak ning vuk bangin”
A siangtho khuapi sungah, Innpite taang mahmah;
Vangliatna ngah a mite, a puansilh uh a tee;
Tua a phate siasak ding, bangmah tum theilo ding;
Vantung mite’ cinna ah, ka om ding hi, keimah.
=== A KUMKUM IN NUAM SEMSEM ===
Key : Ab
Mawhna sung ka om lai-in, Jesuh itna’n hong zong;
A lam dang hehpih na in, Hong kha kik tuu buk dong;
A thuk, a sang hehpihna, Tuipi sang zong thuk zaw;
Vantung sangin zong sang zaw, Ka deih bel hi lo maw.
Sakkik
A kumkum in nuam semsem,
A kum kum in nuam semsem;
Jesuh it-na lian zaw, cing zaw, thukzaw, khumzaw,
A kum-kum in nuam semsem.
Tang lai Judea gam sungah, Jesuh vak kawikawi a;
Hotkhiatna thu thei nuam in, Mi hon hong pai uh a;
Lung tamkham te damsakin, Mittawte vaak sak hi;
A migitna lungsim in, Kei na ngawn hong it hi.
A lamdang hong itna hang, Supna, baina hong thuak;
Singlamteh tungah gimna, Phun lo, pau lo-in thuak;
Tatkhiat sa mi siangte tawh, I aw sang khai ve ni;
Leitung vantung thawnsak in, Ei hong Tanpa phat ni.
=== A KILAWM KONGPITE KIHON CIANG ===
Key : G
Zan khuamialna ah i vakthap nawn kei ding,
A kilawm kong pi kihon ciang;
Pasian khuavak a hihna khua i pai ding,
A kilawm kongpi kihon ciang.
Sakkik
A kilawm kongpi kihon ciang,
A kilawm kongpi kihon ciang;
Tua mun-ah Topa mu in i lung nuam ding,
A kilawm kongpi kihon ciang.
Natna, satna dahnate om nawn lo ding,
A kilawm kongpi kihon ciang;
A pai sa I lawm itte tawh kikhawl ding,
A kilawm kongpi kihon ciang.
Gen khiat zawh loh lawpna kei aa hi ta ding,
A kilawm kongpi kihon ciang;
Amah en in a sianthona ka mu ding,
A kilawm kongpi kihon ciang.
Leitung vangik te’n hong nawngkai sak lo ding,
A kilawm kongpi kihon ciang;
Lungdam tawntungna ah Khris tawh i teng ding,
A kilawm kongpi kihon ciang.
=== A ETLAWMIN TOPA BIA UN ===
Key : Bb
Etlawm tak le siangtho takin Topa bia in,
Amai ah kunin Amin thangsak ni;
A thu mangin kiniamkhiatna tawh va bia in,
Amah phat ni, Ama min Topa hi.
A khe phungah na lungkhamnate va nga in,
Amah’n nang tangin hong puaksak ding hi;
Na thumna hong dawngin nang hong lungnuamsak in,
Ahoih penin hong vaihawmsak ding hi.
Na neihsa piak tawm lua, ci-in kisuang ken la,
A tokhom zuat ding lau ngaihsut kei in;
A etlawm thumanna le a siangtho itna,
Ama tau ah biakpiakna cing hikhin
Lau kawm, liing kawmin tuate i va puak ciangin,
Lungkim takin Topa’n hong sang ding hi;
Dahna, kahnate khempeuh lungdamna suakin,
Launa teng zong lawpna, muanna suak hi.
=== A AW KA THEI ===
Key : Ab
Honpa ka muh theihloh hangin,
Hong hehpih den hi, nisimin;
Amah ka teel tu-in ka nei,
Topa phat un, A aw ka thei.
Sakkik
A aw ka thei, Honpa’ aw hi;
Ka lungsim sung hong nuamsak hi;
Hun simin kei hong hoph hi,
A aw ka thei Topa phat ni!
A mel ka muh loh hangin ah,
Huihpi lak pan A aw ka za;
Tuihual kham in dai pah hilhial;
Ni hong tangin nuam pah silsial.
Thuman, thutak hong genkhia-a,
Muh batloh tawldamna nopna;
Itna, kilemna thugen hi,
Van innpi thu zong hong gen hi.
